# check-project-inbox

Before writing code on any project in `~/projects/`, pull the project owner's WhatsApp messages, images (with AI transcriptions), and voice notes (with AI transcriptions) from the Tokyo server. Shows exactly what the client asked for.

## How It Works

1. Reads `project-mapping.json` in this skill's directory to find WhatsApp JIDs for the current project folder name
2. Runs SSH SQL queries on `root@mycontabo` against `/root/tokyo/life.db`
3. Returns recent messages, image transcriptions, and audio transcriptions grouped by urgency

## Data Model

| Column | Type | Meaning |
|--------|------|---------|
| `content` | TEXT | Message body (text), null for media |
| `transcription` | TEXT | AI-generated description of images or audio transcription |
| `message_type` | TEXT | `text`, `image`, `audio`, `video`, `sticker`, `document` |
| `from_me` | INTEGER | 0 = from contact, 1 = from you (M) |
| `jid` | TEXT | Contact/group ID |
| `sender_name` | TEXT | Display name of sender |
| `timestamp` | INTEGER | Unix epoch |

**Filtering:** Always use `from_me=0` for client messages. Media messages have `transcription` populated by the Cohere model (Mac Transcribe server).

## Canonical Snippets

> **SSH quoting:** Always wrap the full SQL in single quotes on the remote side. Do NOT use heredoc-style `"..."` wrapping — the nested quotes break over SSH. Tested pattern: `ssh root@mycontabo 'sqlite3 ... "SELECT ... WHERE jid='\''<JID>'\'' ..."'`

### Full recent convo (last 7 days, all types)
```bash
ssh root@mycontabo 'sqlite3 -header -column /root/tokyo/life.db "SELECT id, sender_name, message_type, datetime(timestamp,'\''unixepoch'\'','\''localtime'\'') as sent, CASE WHEN message_type='\''text'\'' THEN substr(content,1,200) WHEN transcription IS NOT NULL THEN '\''[Transcription: '\'' || substr(transcription,1,200) || '\'']'\'' ELSE '\''['\'' || message_type || '\'']'\'' END as excerpt FROM whatsapp_messages WHERE jid='\''<JID>'\'' AND from_me=0 AND timestamp > (strftime('\''%s'\'','\''now'\'','\''-7 days'\'')) ORDER BY timestamp DESC LIMIT 40;"'
```

### Client's pending asks (unanswered by you)
```bash
ssh root@mycontabo 'sqlite3 -header -column /root/tokyo/life.db "SELECT id, sender_name, message_type, datetime(timestamp,'\''unixepoch'\'','\''localtime'\'') as sent, content, transcription FROM whatsapp_messages WHERE jid='\''<JID>'\'' AND from_me=0 AND timestamp > (strftime('\''%s'\'','\''now'\'','\''-7 days'\'')) AND id > (SELECT COALESCE(MAX(id),0) FROM whatsapp_messages WHERE jid='\''<JID>'\'' AND from_me=1) ORDER BY timestamp DESC LIMIT 15;"'
```

### Images with transcriptions (last 14 days)
```bash
ssh root@mycontabo 'sqlite3 -header -column /root/tokyo/life.db "SELECT id, sender_name, datetime(timestamp,'\''unixepoch'\'','\''localtime'\'') as sent, transcription FROM whatsapp_messages WHERE jid='\''<JID>'\'' AND from_me=0 AND message_type='\''image'\'' AND transcription IS NOT NULL AND timestamp > (strftime('\''%s'\'','\''now'\'','\''-14 days'\'')) ORDER BY timestamp DESC LIMIT 20;"'
```

### Voice notes with transcriptions (last 14 days)
```bash
ssh root@mycontabo 'sqlite3 -header -column /root/tokyo/life.db "SELECT id, sender_name, datetime(timestamp,'\''unixepoch'\'','\''localtime'\'') as sent, transcription, duration_seconds, wpm FROM whatsapp_messages WHERE jid='\''<JID>'\'' AND from_me=0 AND message_type='\''audio'\'' AND transcription IS NOT NULL AND timestamp > (strftime('\''%s'\'','\''now'\'','\''-14 days'\'')) ORDER BY timestamp DESC LIMIT 20;"'
```

### Quick unread count since your last reply
```bash
ssh root@mycontabo 'sqlite3 -header -column /root/tokyo/life.db "SELECT COUNT(*) AS unread_msgs, (SELECT datetime(timestamp,'\''unixepoch'\'','\''localtime'\'') FROM whatsapp_messages WHERE jid='\''<JID>'\'' AND from_me=1 ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 1) AS your_last_reply FROM whatsapp_messages WHERE jid='\''<JID>'\'' AND from_me=0 AND id > COALESCE((SELECT MAX(id) FROM whatsapp_messages WHERE jid='\''<JID>'\'' AND from_me=1),0);"'
```

## Output Format

Always present results grouped as:

```
## Project: <label> — <contact_name>

### Unread since your last reply: <count>

### Pending asks (unanswered)
| Time | Content |
|------|---------|
| ... | ... |

### Recent images (with transcriptions)
| Time | What's shown |
|------|-------------|
| ... | ... |

### Recent voice notes (with transcriptions)
| Time | Duration | WPM | What they said |
|------|----------|-----|----------------|
| ... | ... | ... | ... |

### Recent text messages
| Time | Message |
|------|---------|
| ... | ... |
```

## Project Mapping

The mapping between project directory names and WhatsApp JIDs lives in `project-mapping.json` in this skill's directory. To add a new project, edit that file. Example entry:

```json
{
  "folder_name": {
    "label": "Project Name",
    "contacts": [
      { "jid": "<jid>", "name": "<name>", "role": "owner", "is_group": 0 }
    ]
  }
}
```

Find a JID by searching the server:
```bash
ssh root@mycontabo "sqlite3 /root/tokyo/life.db \"SELECT jid, sender_name, COUNT(*) FROM whatsapp_messages WHERE from_me=0 AND sender_name LIKE '%<name>%' GROUP BY jid ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC LIMIT 5;\""
```

## Common Mistakes

- **Skipping images/voice notes** — they carry critical feedback in Arabic via transcriptions
- **Only checking text messages** — clients often send screenshots and voice notes that contain the actual asks
- **Not checking the mapping file first** — before querying, always read `project-mapping.json`
- **Querying without date filter** — always limit to last 7-14 days to avoid huge results
- **Forgetting groups** — some projects use group chats (is_group=1), others use 1:1

# Requesting Code Review

Dispatch superpowers:code-reviewer subagent to catch issues before they cascade. The reviewer gets precisely crafted context for evaluation — never your session's history. This keeps the reviewer focused on the work product, not your thought process, and preserves your own context for continued work.

**Core principle:** Review early, review often.

## When to Request Review

**Mandatory:**
- After each task in subagent-driven development
- After completing major feature
- Before merge to main

**Optional but valuable:**
- When stuck (fresh perspective)
- Before refactoring (baseline check)
- After fixing complex bug

## How to Request

**1. Get git SHAs:**
```bash
BASE_SHA=$(git rev-parse HEAD~1)  # or origin/main
HEAD_SHA=$(git rev-parse HEAD)
```

**2. Dispatch code-reviewer subagent:**

Use Task tool with superpowers:code-reviewer type, fill template at `code-reviewer.md`

**Placeholders:**
- `{WHAT_WAS_IMPLEMENTED}` - What you just built
- `{PLAN_OR_REQUIREMENTS}` - What it should do
- `{BASE_SHA}` - Starting commit
- `{HEAD_SHA}` - Ending commit
- `{DESCRIPTION}` - Brief summary

**3. Act on feedback:**
- Fix Critical issues immediately
- Fix Important issues before proceeding
- Note Minor issues for later
- Push back if reviewer is wrong (with reasoning)

## Example

```
[Just completed Task 2: Add verification function]

You: Let me request code review before proceeding.

BASE_SHA=$(git log --oneline | grep "Task 1" | head -1 | awk '{print $1}')
HEAD_SHA=$(git rev-parse HEAD)

[Dispatch superpowers:code-reviewer subagent]
  WHAT_WAS_IMPLEMENTED: Verification and repair functions for conversation index
  PLAN_OR_REQUIREMENTS: Task 2 from docs/superpowers/plans/deployment-plan.md
  BASE_SHA: a7981ec
  HEAD_SHA: 3df7661
  DESCRIPTION: Added verifyIndex() and repairIndex() with 4 issue types

[Subagent returns]:
  Strengths: Clean architecture, real tests
  Issues:
    Important: Missing progress indicators
    Minor: Magic number (100) for reporting interval
  Assessment: Ready to proceed

You: [Fix progress indicators]
[Continue to Task 3]
```

## Integration with Workflows

**Subagent-Driven Development:**
- Review after EACH task
- Catch issues before they compound
- Fix before moving to next task

**Executing Plans:**
- Review after each batch (3 tasks)
- Get feedback, apply, continue

**Ad-Hoc Development:**
- Review before merge
- Review when stuck

## Red Flags

**Never:**
- Skip review because "it's simple"
- Ignore Critical issues
- Proceed with unfixed Important issues
- Argue with valid technical feedback

**If reviewer wrong:**
- Push back with technical reasoning
- Show code/tests that prove it works
- Request clarification

See template at: requesting-code-review/code-reviewer.md

## Instruction Priority

Superpowers skills override default system prompt behavior, but **user instructions always take precedence**:

1. **User's explicit instructions** (CLAUDE.md, GEMINI.md, AGENTS.md, direct requests) — highest priority
2. **Superpowers skills** — override default system behavior where they conflict
3. **Default system prompt** — lowest priority

If CLAUDE.md, GEMINI.md, or AGENTS.md says "don't use TDD" and a skill says "always use TDD," follow the user's instructions. The user is in control.

## How to Access Skills

**In Claude Code:** Use the `Skill` tool. When you invoke a skill, its content is loaded and presented to you—follow it directly. Never use the Read tool on skill files.

**In Copilot CLI:** Use the `skill` tool. Skills are auto-discovered from installed plugins. The `skill` tool works the same as Claude Code's `Skill` tool.

**In Gemini CLI:** Skills activate via the `activate_skill` tool. Gemini loads skill metadata at session start and activates the full content on demand.

**In other environments:** Check your platform's documentation for how skills are loaded.

## Platform Adaptation

Skills use Claude Code tool names. Non-CC platforms: see `references/copilot-tools.md` (Copilot CLI), `references/codex-tools.md` (Codex) for tool equivalents. Gemini CLI users get the tool mapping loaded automatically via GEMINI.md.

# Using Skills

## The Rule

**Invoke relevant or requested skills BEFORE any response or action.** Even a 1% chance a skill might apply means that you should invoke the skill to check. If an invoked skill turns out to be wrong for the situation, you don't need to use it.

```dot
digraph skill_flow {
    "User message received" [shape=doublecircle];
    "About to EnterPlanMode?" [shape=doublecircle];
    "Already brainstormed?" [shape=diamond];
    "Invoke brainstorming skill" [shape=box];
    "Might any skill apply?" [shape=diamond];
    "Invoke Skill tool" [shape=box];
    "Announce: 'Using [skill] to [purpose]'" [shape=box];
    "Has checklist?" [shape=diamond];
    "Create TodoWrite todo per item" [shape=box];
    "Follow skill exactly" [shape=box];
    "Respond (including clarifications)" [shape=doublecircle];

    "About to EnterPlanMode?" -> "Already brainstormed?";
    "Already brainstormed?" -> "Invoke brainstorming skill" [label="no"];
    "Already brainstormed?" -> "Might any skill apply?" [label="yes"];
    "Invoke brainstorming skill" -> "Might any skill apply?";

    "User message received" -> "Might any skill apply?";
    "Might any skill apply?" -> "Invoke Skill tool" [label="yes, even 1%"];
    "Might any skill apply?" -> "Respond (including clarifications)" [label="definitely not"];
    "Invoke Skill tool" -> "Announce: 'Using [skill] to [purpose]'";
    "Announce: 'Using [skill] to [purpose]'" -> "Has checklist?";
    "Has checklist?" -> "Create TodoWrite todo per item" [label="yes"];
    "Has checklist?" -> "Follow skill exactly" [label="no"];
    "Create TodoWrite todo per item" -> "Follow skill exactly";
}
```

## Red Flags

These thoughts mean STOP—you're rationalizing:

| Thought | Reality |
|---------|---------|
| "This is just a simple question" | Questions are tasks. Check for skills. |
| "I need more context first" | Skill check comes BEFORE clarifying questions. |
| "Let me explore the codebase first" | Skills tell you HOW to explore. Check first. |
| "I can check git/files quickly" | Files lack conversation context. Check for skills. |
| "Let me gather information first" | Skills tell you HOW to gather information. |
| "This doesn't need a formal skill" | If a skill exists, use it. |
| "I remember this skill" | Skills evolve. Read current version. |
| "This doesn't count as a task" | Action = task. Check for skills. |
| "The skill is overkill" | Simple things become complex. Use it. |
| "I'll just do this one thing first" | Check BEFORE doing anything. |
| "This feels productive" | Undisciplined action wastes time. Skills prevent this. |
| "I know what that means" | Knowing the concept ≠ using the skill. Invoke it. |

## Skill Priority

When multiple skills could apply, use this order:

1. **Process skills first** (brainstorming, debugging) - these determine HOW to approach the task
2. **Implementation skills second** (frontend-design, mcp-builder) - these guide execution

"Let's build X" → brainstorming first, then implementation skills.
"Fix this bug" → debugging first, then domain-specific skills.

## Skill Types

**Rigid** (TDD, debugging): Follow exactly. Don't adapt away discipline.

**Flexible** (patterns): Adapt principles to context.

The skill itself tells you which.

## User Instructions

Instructions say WHAT, not HOW. "Add X" or "Fix Y" doesn't mean skip workflows.

<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Seller;

use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use App\Models\Category;
use App\Models\Stock;
use App\Models\Store;
use App\Services\StorageService;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Builder;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Auth;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;
use Illuminate\Support\Str;

/**
 * Seller-facing Blade CRUD for products (backed by the `stocks` table).
 *
 * Spec: specs/006-seller-experience/spec.md § Slice A.
 * Replaces the JSON API\SellerProductController binding for /seller/products/*.
 * Scoped strictly to the authenticated seller's own store.
 */
class ProductController extends Controller
{
    /**
     * Resolve the seller's store or send them to the create-store flow.
     *
     * @return \App\Models\Store|\Illuminate\Http\RedirectResponse
     */
    private function resolveStore()
    {
        $store = Store::where('user_id', Auth::id())->first();

        if (! $store) {
            $target = \Illuminate\Support\Facades\Route::has('store.request.create')
                ? route('store.request.create')
                : route('seller.dashboard');

            return redirect($target)->with('error', __('messages.no_store_found'));
        }

        return $store;
    }

    /**
     * Display a paginated list of the seller's products with search + category filter.
     */
    public function index(Request $request)
    {
        $storeOrRedirect = $this->resolveStore();
        if (! $storeOrRedirect instanceof Store) {
            return $storeOrRedirect;
        }
        $store = $storeOrRedirect;

        $q          = trim((string) $request->input('q', ''));
        $categoryId = $request->input('category_id');

        $query = Stock::query()
            ->with(['category', 'productImages'])
            ->where('store_id', $store->id)
            ->where('is_deleted', false);

        if ($q !== '') {
            $query->where(function (Builder $b) use ($q) {
                $b->where('product_name_en', 'like', "%{$q}%")
                  ->orWhere('product_name_ar', 'like', "%{$q}%");
            });
        }

        if (! empty($categoryId)) {
            $query->where('category_id', $categoryId);
        }

        $products = $query->latest()->paginate(20)->withQueryString();

        $categories = Category::orderBy('category_name_en')->get();

        return view('seller.products.index', compact('products', 'categories', 'q', 'categoryId', 'store'));
    }

    /**
     * Show the form to create a new product.
     */
    public function create()
    {
        $storeOrRedirect = $this->resolveStore();
        if (! $storeOrRedirect instanceof Store) {
            return $storeOrRedirect;
        }
        $store = $storeOrRedirect;

        $categories = Category::orderBy('category_name_en')->get();
        $product = new Stock(); // empty model so the partial can dot-access fields without isset()

        return view('seller.products.create', compact('product', 'categories', 'store'));
    }

    /**
     * Persist a new product scoped to the seller's store.
     */
    public function store(Request $request)
    {
        $storeOrRedirect = $this->resolveStore();
        if (! $storeOrRedirect instanceof Store) {
            return $storeOrRedirect;
        }
        $store = $storeOrRedirect;

        $validated = $request->validate([
            'product_name_en'         => 'required|string|max:255',
            'product_name_ar'         => 'nullable|string|max:255',
            'description'             => 'nullable|string|max:5000',
            'description_ar'          => 'nullable|string|max:5000',
            'category_id'             => 'required|exists:categories,id',
            'current_sale_unit_price' => 'required|numeric|min:0',
            'quantity'                => 'required|integer|min:0',
            'is_active'               => 'nullable|boolean',
            'product_image'           => 'nullable|image|max:5120', // 5 MB
        ]);

        try {
            DB::beginTransaction();

            $stock = new Stock();
            $stock->store_id = $store->id;
            $stock->user_id  = Auth::id();
            $stock->company_id = $store->company_id ?? Auth::user()->company_id ?? null;
            $stock->branch_id  = $store->branch_id ?? Auth::user()->branch_id ?? null;
            $stock->category_id = $validated['category_id'];
            $stock->product_name_en = $validated['product_name_en'];
            $stock->product_name_ar = $validated['product_name_ar'] ?? null;
            $stock->description     = $validated['description'] ?? null;
            $stock->description_ar  = $validated['description_ar'] ?? null;
            $stock->current_sale_unit_price = $validated['current_sale_unit_price'];
            $stock->quantity        = $validated['quantity'];
            $stock->type            = 'Finished Product';
            $stock->slug            = Str::slug($validated['product_name_en']) . '-' . Str::random(6);
            // Direct attribute assignment — is_active/is_deleted live on the table but not in $fillable.
            $stock->is_active  = $request->boolean('is_active', true) ? 1 : 0;
            $stock->is_deleted = false;

            if ($request->hasFile('product_image')) {
                $file = $request->file('product_image');
                $path = 'stocks/' . $store->id . '/' . time() . '_' . Str::random(8) . '.' . $file->getClientOriginalExtension();
                $stored = app(StorageService::class)->putFile($file, $path);
                if ($stored !== false) {
                    $stock->image = $path;
                }
            }

            $stock->save();

            DB::commit();
        } catch (\Throwable $e) {
            DB::rollBack();
            Log::error('Seller\\ProductController::store failed', [
                'store_id' => $store->id,
                'error'    => $e->getMessage(),
            ]);

            return back()->withInput()->with('error', __('messages.something_went_wrong'));
        }

        return redirect()->route('seller.products.show', $stock->id)
            ->with('success', __('messages.product_saved'));
    }

    /**
     * Display a single product.
     */
    public function show($id)
    {
        $storeOrRedirect = $this->resolveStore();
        if (! $storeOrRedirect instanceof Store) {
            return $storeOrRedirect;
        }
        $store = $storeOrRedirect;

        $product = Stock::with(['category', 'productImages'])
            ->where('store_id', $store->id)
            ->where('is_deleted', false)
            ->find($id);

        if (! $product) {
            abort(403);
        }

        return view('seller.products.show', compact('product', 'store'));
    }

    /**

    public function edit($id)

        $storeOrRedirect = $this->resolveStore();

        return view('seller.products.edit', compact('product', 'categories', 'store'));
    }

<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Admin;

use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use App\Http\Requests\BulkVariantRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\UpdateVariantInventoryRequest;
use App\Models\Currency;
use App\Models\InventoryHistory;
use App\Models\ProductVariant;
use App\Models\Stock;
use App\Models\VariantColor;
use App\Models\VariantFabric;
use App\Models\VariantSize;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Session;

class ProductVariantController extends Controller
{
    protected function getCurrencySymbol()
    {
        return Currency::getCurrencySymbol();
    }

    public function index($stock_id)
    {
        $stock = Stock::findOrFail($stock_id);

        // Get variants with their relationships
        $variants = ProductVariant::where('stock_id', $stock_id)
            ->with(['size', 'fabric', 'color'])
            ->get()
            ->groupBy(function ($variant) {
                // Group by base SKU (remove the size/color/fabric codes)
                return preg_replace('/-[^-]+-[^-]+-[^-]+$/', '', $variant->sku);
            })
            ->map(function ($groupedVariants) {
                $firstVariant = $groupedVariants->first();
                // Get base name by removing the attribute parts
                $firstVariant->base_name = preg_replace('/\s*-\s*[^-]+\s*-\s*[^-]+$/', '', $firstVariant->name);
                $firstVariant->total_quantity = $groupedVariants->sum('quantity');
                $firstVariant->all_sizes = $groupedVariants->pluck('size')->flatten()->unique('id')->filter();
                $firstVariant->all_fabrics = $groupedVariants->pluck('fabric')->flatten()->unique('id')->filter();
                $firstVariant->all_colors = $groupedVariants->pluck('color')->flatten()->unique('id')->filter();
                $firstVariant->grouped_variants = $groupedVariants;

                return $firstVariant;
            })
            ->values();

        return view('admin.variants.index', compact('variants', 'stock'));
    }

    public function create($stock_id)
    {
        $currency_symbol = $this->getCurrencySymbol();

        $stock = Stock::findOrFail($stock_id);

        return view('admin.variants.create', compact('stock', 'currency_symbol'));
    }

    public function store(Request $request, $stock_id)
    {
        $validated = $request->validate([
            'name' => 'required|string|max:255',
            'sku' => 'required|string|unique:product_variants,sku',
            'price' => 'required|numeric|min:0',
            'quantity' => 'required|integer|min:0',
            'attribute_keys' => 'nullable|array',
            'attribute_values' => 'nullable|array',
            'is_default' => 'boolean',
            'is_active' => 'boolean',
        ]);

        $stock = Stock::findOrFail($stock_id);

        // Combine attribute keys and values into an associative array
        $attributes = [];
        if (! empty($validated['attribute_keys']) && ! empty($validated['attribute_values'])) {
            foreach ($validated['attribute_keys'] as $index => $key) {
                if (! empty($key) && ! empty($validated['attribute_values'][$index])) {
                    $attributes[$key] = $validated['attribute_values'][$index];
                }
            }
        }

        // Remove the separate attribute arrays and add the combined attributes
        unset($validated['attribute_keys'], $validated['attribute_values']);
        $validated['attributes'] = json_encode($attributes);

        $variant = new ProductVariant($validated);
        $variant->stock_id = $stock_id;
        $variant->save();

        // Attach sizes, fabrics, and colors to the variant using their IDs
        if ($request->has('sizes')) {
            $variant->sizes()->attach($request->input('sizes'));
        }
        if ($request->has('fabrics')) {
            $variant->fabrics()->attach($request->input('fabrics'));
        }
        if ($request->has('selected_colors')) {
            $variant->colors()->attach($request->input('selected_colors'));
        }

        Session::flash('message', __('Variant added successfully'));

        if ($request->filled('redirect_to') && str_starts_with($request->input('redirect_to'), url('/'))) {
            return redirect($request->input('redirect_to'));
        }

        return redirect()->route('admin.variants.index', $stock_id);
    }

    public function edit($stock_id, $variant_id)
    {
        $currency_symbol = $this->getCurrencySymbol();
        $stock = Stock::findOrFail($stock_id);
        $variant = ProductVariant::with(['size', 'fabric', 'color'])->findOrFail($variant_id);

        // Get all available sizes, fabrics, and colors
        $sizes = VariantSize::orderBy('name')->get();
        $fabrics = VariantFabric::orderBy('name')->get();
        $colors = VariantColor::orderBy('name')->get();

        return view('admin.variants.edit', compact('variant', 'stock', 'currency_symbol', 'sizes', 'fabrics', 'colors'));
    }

    public function update(Request $request, $stock_id, $variant_id)
    {
        $validated = $request->validate([
            'sku' => 'required|string|unique:product_variants,sku,'.$variant_id,
            'price' => 'required|numeric|min:0',
            'quantity' => 'required|integer|min:0',
            'size_id' => 'required|exists:variant_sizes,id',
            'fabric_id' => 'required|exists:variant_fabrics,id',
            'color_id' => 'required|exists:variant_colors,id',
            'is_default' => 'boolean',
            'is_active' => 'boolean',
        ]);

        DB::beginTransaction();
        try {
            $variant = ProductVariant::findOrFail($variant_id);
            $oldData = $variant->toArray();

            // Update basic variant information
            $variant->update([
                'sku' => $validated['sku'],
                'price' => $validated['price'],
                'quantity' => $validated['quantity'],
                'is_default' => $request->has('is_default'),
                'is_active' => $request->has('is_active'),
            ]);

            // If this variant is set as default, remove default status from other variants
            if ($request->has('is_default')) {
                ProductVariant::where('stock_id', $stock_id)
                    ->where('id', '!=', $variant->id)
                    ->update(['is_default' => false]);
            }

            // Update variant attributes
            DB::table('variant_attribute_values')->updateOrInsert(
                ['variant_id' => $variant->id],
                [
                    'size_id' => $validated['size_id'],
                    'fabric_id' => $validated['fabric_id'],
                    'color_id' => $validated['color_id'],
                    'updated_at' => now(),
                ]
            );

            // Update variant name based on attributes
            $size = DB::table('variant_sizes')->where('id', $validated['size_id'])->first();
            $fabric = DB::table('variant_fabrics')->where('id', $validated['fabric_id'])->first();
            $color = DB::table('variant_colors')->where('id', $validated['color_id'])->first();

            $variantName = sprintf(
                '%s - %s - %s - %s',
                $variant->stock->product_name,
                $size->name,
                $fabric->name,
                $color->name
            );

            $variant->update(['name' => $variantName]);

            // Log the update
            \Log::info('Variant updated', [
                'variant_id' => $variant->id,
                'old_data' => $oldData,
                'new_data' => array_merge(
                    $variant->fresh()->toArray(),
                    [
                        'size_id' => $validated['size_id'],
                        'fabric_id' => $validated['fabric_id'],
                        'color_id' => $validated['color_id'],
                        'is_active' => $request->has('is_active'),
                        'is_default' => $request->has('is_default'),
                    ]
                ),
            ]);

            DB::commit();
            Session::flash('message', __('messages.variant_updated_successfully'));

            if ($request->filled('redirect_to') && str_starts_with($request->input('redirect_to'), url('/'))) {
                return redirect($request->input('redirect_to'));
            }

            return redirect()->route('admin.variants.index', $stock_id);

        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            DB::rollback();
            \Log::error('Failed to update variant: '.$e->getMessage(), [
                'variant_id' => $variant_id,
                'error' => $e,
                'request_data' => $request->all(),
            ]);

            Session::flash('error', __('messages.failed_to_update_variant'));

            return back()->withInput();
        }
    }

    // delete-Variant

    {
        $variant = ProductVariant::findOrFail($id);
        $variant->delete();

        Session::flash('message', __('Variant deleted successfully'));

        return redirect()->route('admin.variants.index', $variant->stock_id);
    }

            return redirect($request->input('redirect_to'));
        }

        return redirect()->route('admin.variants.index', $stock_id);
    }

        $action = $request->input('action');

<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Admin;

use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use App\Models\ProductVariant;
use App\Models\Stock;
use App\Models\VariantColor;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class VariantInventoryController extends Controller
{
    /**
     * Display the inventory management page for a product.
     *
     * @param  Stock  $stock_id  The stock model (auto-resolved by Laravel)
     * @return \Illuminate\View\View
     */
    public function index(Stock $stock_id)
    {
        // Rename the variable to match the expected name in views
        $stock = $stock_id;

        // Get all product images with their color groups
        $productImages = DB::table('product_images')
            ->where('stock_id', $stock->id)
            ->whereNotNull('color_group')
            ->select('color_group', 'color_hex')
            ->distinct()
            ->get()
            ->map(function ($item) {
                // Convert to array to avoid collection property access issues
                return (array) $item;
            });

        // Get all variants for this stock with optimized eager loading
        $variants = ProductVariant::where('stock_id', $stock->id)
            ->with(['size', 'color', 'fabric', 'images'])
            ->orderBy('created_at', 'desc')
            ->get();

        // Get primary images for each color group
        $primaryGroupImages = DB::table('product_color_groups')
            ->where('stock_id', $stock->id)
            ->pluck('primary_image_id', 'color_group')
            ->toArray();

        // Get all product images
        $allImages = DB::table('product_images')
            ->where('stock_id', $stock->id)
            ->get()
            ->keyBy('id');

        // Create color groups based on product images
        $imageColorGroups = collect();
        foreach ($productImages as $group) {
            $colorGroup = $group['color_group'] ?? null;
            if (! $colorGroup) {
                continue;
            }

            $imageColorGroups[$colorGroup] = [
                'name' => $colorGroup,
                'color_hex' => $group['color_hex'] ?? null,
                'variants' => collect(),
                'primary_image_id' => $primaryGroupImages[$colorGroup] ?? null,
                'primary_image' => isset($primaryGroupImages[$colorGroup]) ? $allImages[$primaryGroupImages[$colorGroup]] : null,
            ];
        }

        // Assign variants to image color groups based on their associated images
        foreach ($variants as $variant) {
            $assigned = false;

            // Check if variant has images and assign to matching color group
            if ($variant->images && $variant->images->isNotEmpty()) {
                foreach ($variant->images as $image) {
                    if (! empty($image->color_group) && isset($imageColorGroups[$image->color_group])) {
                        $imageColorGroups[$image->color_group]['variants']->push($variant);
                        $assigned = true;
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }

            // If no match with images, try to match by color
            if (! $assigned && $variant->color) {
                // Make sure variant color has a hex_code property before attempting to match
                $variantHexCode = null;

                // Check if color is an object with hex_code property
                if (is_object($variant->color) && property_exists($variant->color, 'hex_code')) {
                    $variantHexCode = $variant->color->hex_code;
                }
                // If color is an array, check for hex_code key
                elseif (is_array($variant->color) && isset($variant->color['hex_code'])) {
                    $variantHexCode = $variant->color['hex_code'];
                }

                // Only proceed with matching if we have a valid hex code
                if ($variantHexCode) {
                    foreach ($imageColorGroups as $groupName => $group) {
                        // Make sure group has a valid color_hex value before comparing
                        if (isset($group['color_hex']) && ! empty($group['color_hex']) && $group['color_hex'] == $variantHexCode) {
                            $imageColorGroups[$groupName]['variants']->push($variant);
                            $assigned = true;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            // If still no match, add to ungrouped
            if (! $assigned) {
                if (! isset($imageColorGroups['ungrouped'])) {
                    $imageColorGroups['ungrouped'] = [
                        'name' => 'Ungrouped',
                        'color_hex' => null,
                        'variants' => collect(),
                        'primary_image_id' => null,
                        'primary_image' => null,
                    ];
                }
                $imageColorGroups['ungrouped']['variants']->push($variant);
            }
        }

        // Get unique colors used by this product
        $colors = VariantColor::whereHas('variants', function ($query) use ($stock) {
            $query->where('stock_id', $stock->id);
        })->get();

        return view('admin.products.inventory.index', [
            'stock' => $stock,
            'variants' => $variants,
            'colorGroups' => $imageColorGroups,
            'colors' => $colors,
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * Update inventory for a specific variant.
     *
     * @param  int  $variant_id
     * @return \Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse
     */
    public function updateInventory(Request $request, $variant_id)
    {
        $request->validate([
            'quantity' => 'required|integer|min:0',
            'price' => 'required|numeric|min:0',
        ]);

        try {
            $variant = ProductVariant::findOrFail($variant_id);
            $stock = $variant->stock;

            $variant->update([
                'price' => $request->input('price'),
                'quantity' => $request->input('quantity'),
            ]);

            // Clear the stock's total quantity cache
            $this->clearStockQuantityCache($stock);

            return response()->json([
                'success' => true,
                'message' => __('messages.inventory_updated'),
                'variant' => $variant,
            ]);
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            Log::error('Error updating variant inventory: '.$e->getMessage());

            return response()->json([
                'success' => false,
                'message' => __('messages.update_failed'),
            ], 500);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Bulk update inventory for multiple variants.
     *
     * @return \Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse
     */
    public function bulkUpdate(Request $request, Stock $stock_id)
    {
        // Rename the variable to match the expected name in views
        $stock = $stock_id;

        $request->validate([
            'variants' => 'required|array',
            'variants.*.id' => 'required|exists:product_variants,id',
            'variants.*.quantity' => 'required|integer|min:0',
            'variants.*.price' => 'required|numeric|min:0',
        ]);

        try {
            DB::beginTransaction();

            foreach ($request->variants as $variantData) {
                ProductVariant::where('id', $variantData['id'])
                    ->update([
                        'quantity' => $variantData['quantity'],
                        'price' => $variantData['price'],
                    ]);
            }

            DB::commit();

            // Clear the stock's total quantity cache
            $this->clearStockQuantityCache($stock);

            return response()->json([
                'success' => true,
                'message' => __('messages.inventory_bulk_updated'),
            ]);
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            DB::rollBack();
            Log::error('Error bulk updating inventory: '.$e->getMessage());

            return response()->json([
                'success' => false,
                'message' => __('messages.update_failed'),
            ], 500);
        }
    }

    public function updateColorInventory(Request $request, Stock $stock_id, $color)

            // Update all variants with this color for this stock
            $variants = ProductVariant::whereHas('color', function ($query) use ($color) {
                $query->where('hex_code', $color);

<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Admin;

use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use App\Models\AccountActivity;
use App\Models\AccountControl;
use App\Models\AccountHead;

use App\Services\LanguageService;

class StockController extends Controller
{
    private $languageService;

    private $dateFilter;

    private $searchService;

    protected $imageService;

    private $revalidationService;

    public function __construct(
        LanguageService $languageService, 
        DateFilterService $dateFilter, 
        SearchService $searchService, 
        ImageService $imageService,
        NextJsRevalidationService $revalidationService
    ) {
        $this->languageService = $languageService;
        $this->dateFilter = $dateFilter;
        $this->searchService = $searchService;
        $this->imageService = $imageService;
        $this->revalidationService = $revalidationService;
    }

    public function index(Request $request)
    {

        $productName = $this->languageService->resolveLocalizedFieldName('product_name');
        $authUser = Auth::user();
        if ($authUser->roles[0]->name == 'super-admin') {
            $stocks = Stock::with(['category', 'user', 'variants'])
                ->where([
                    'is_deleted' => 0,
                ]);
        } else {
            $stocks = Stock::with(['category', 'user'])
                ->where([
                    'company_id' => Auth::user()->company_id,
                    'branch_id' => Auth::user()->branch_id,
                    'is_deleted' => 0,
                ]);
        }
        // Apply search
        $stocks = $this->searchService->applySearch($request, $stocks, [$productName, 'barcode'], []);

        // Apply type filter
        if ($request->filled('type')) {
            $stocks->whereRaw('LOWER(type) = ?', [strtolower($request->type)]);
        }

        // Apply date filter
        if ($request->filled('dateFilter')) {
            $stocks = $this->dateFilter->applyDateFilter($stocks, $request->dateFilter, 'created_at');
        }

        // Apply pagination
        $stocks = $stocks->latest()->paginate(10);

        return view('admin.includes.stocks.stocks', compact('stocks'));
    }

    public function create()
    {
        $parentCategories = Category::where('parent_id', 0)->get();
        $units = Unit::where('status', 1)->get();

        return view('admin.includes.stocks.create')->with(compact(['parentCategories', 'units']));
    }

    {

        $productName = $this->languageService->resolveLocalizedFieldName('product_name');
        $description = $this->languageService->resolveLocalizedFieldName('description');

                'category_id' => 'required',

            ]);
            Log::info('Stock validation passed.'); // ADDED FOR DEBUGGING
        } catch (\Illuminate\Validation\ValidationException $e) {
            Log::error('Stock validation failed.', ['errors' => $e->errors(), 'request_all' => $request->except(['product_image'])]); // ADDED FOR DEBUGGING
            // Re-throw the exception to let Laravel handle the redirect with errors

            $stock->$productName = $request->$productName;
            $stock->type = 'Finished Product';
            $stock->barcode = $request->barcode;
            $stock->$description = $request->$description;
            $stock->quantity = $request->quantity;
            $stock->current_sale_unit_price = $request->current_sale_unit_price;
            $stock->current_purchase_unit_price = $request->current_purchase_unit_price;
            $stock->allowtax = $request->allowtax == 1 ? 1 : 0;

            $stock->is_active = 1;

            // Save stock first to get ID
            $stock->save();

            // Handle image upload
            if ($request->hasFile('product_image')) {
                $image = Image::make($request->file('product_image'))
                    ->resize(1200, null, function ($constraint) {
                        $constraint->aspectRatio();
                        $constraint->upsize();
                    });

                // Only encode as webp if supported
                if (function_exists('imagewebp')) {
                    $image->encode('webp', config('app.image_quality', 75));
                } else {
                    $image->encode('jpg', config('app.image_quality', 75));
                }

                $stock->image = $this->handleImageUpload($request, $stock, $request->$productName);
            }

            $this->addInitialStock($stock);

            DB::commit();

            // Trigger Next.js revalidation
            $category = Category::find($stock->category_id);
            $this->revalidationService->revalidateProduct($stock->id, $category->slug ?? null);

            Log::info('Stock created successfully', [
                'stock_id' => $stock->id,
                'image_path' => $stock->image ?? 'no_image',
            ]);

            Session::flash('message', __('messages.stock_added_successfully'));

            // Check if this is an AJAX request for inline confirmation
            if ($request->expectsJson() || $request->ajax()) {
                return response()->json([
                    'success' => true,
                    'message' => __('messages.stock_created_successfully'),
                    'stock' => [
                        'id' => $stock->id,
                        'product_name' => $stock->product_name_en ?? $stock->product_name_ar,
                    ],
                    'redirect_url' => 'https://pro.beldify.com/en/admin/products/' . $stock->id . '/images',
                    'stocks_url' => url('stocks')
                ]);
            }

            // Fallback to redirect for non-AJAX requests
            return redirect()->route('stocks.upload-confirmation', ['id' => $stock->id]);
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            DB::rollBack();
            Log::error('Stock creation failed: '.$e->getMessage(), [
                'exception' => $e,
                'request_data' => $request->except(['product_image']),
            ]);
            Session::flash('error', __('messages.stock_creation_failed'));

            return redirect()->back()->withInput();
        }
    }

    public function uploadConfirmation($id)
    {
        $stock = Stock::findOrFail($id);
        return view('admin.includes.stocks.upload-confirmation', compact('stock'));
    }

    public function edit($id)
    {
        $stock = Stock::find($id);
        $parentCategories = Category::where('parent_id', 0)->get();
        $units = Unit::where('status', 1)->get();

        return view('admin.includes.stocks.update')->with(compact(['stock', 'parentCategories', 'units']));
    }

    /**
     * Display the specified resource.
     *
     * @param  int  $id
     * @return \Illuminate\Http\Response
     */
    public function show($id)
    {
        $stock = Stock::with(['category', 'variants', 'variants.images'])->findOrFail($id);

        // Group variants by color for better organization
        $variantsByColor = $stock->variants->groupBy(function ($variant) {
            $parts = explode(' / ', $variant->name);

            return trim($parts[0] ?? 'Unknown');
        });

        return view('admin.includes.stocks.details', [
            'stock' => $stock,
            'variantsByColor' => $variantsByColor,
        ]);
    }

<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Admin;

use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use App\Models\ProductImage;

class ProductImageController extends Controller

    /**
     * Display a listing of the product images.
     */
    public function index(Request $request, Stock $stock_id)
    {
        // Rename variable to match expected name in views
        $stock = $stock_id;
        $images = collect();

        // Get images from product_images table
        $query = $stock->images()
            ->orderBy('is_primary', 'desc')
            ->orderBy('sort_order');

        // If user is not admin, only show images they own
        /** @var User|null $user */
        $user = auth()->user();
        if ($user && ! $user->hasRole('admin') && ! $user->hasRole('super-admin')) {
            // Only show images for products owned by the current user
            if ($stock->user_id != auth()->id()) {
                $query->where('user_id', auth()->id());
            }
        }

        $productImages = $query->get();

        if ($productImages->isNotEmpty()) {
            $images = $productImages;
        } elseif ($stock->image) {
            // If no product images but stock has legacy image, create a virtual image object
            $images->push((object) [
                'id' => 0,
                'image_path' => (strpos($stock->image, 'http') === 0) ? $stock->image : 'stocks/'.$stock->image,
                'is_primary' => true,
                'alt_text' => $stock->product_name_en,
                'sort_order' => 0,
            ]);
        }

        // Get color hex value if color_group parameter is provided
        $colorHex = null;
        if ($request->has('color_group')) {
            $colorGroup = $request->get('color_group');
            // Find the color hex from product images with this color group
            $imageWithColor = ProductImage::where('stock_id', $stock->id)
                ->where('color_group', $colorGroup)
                ->whereNotNull('color_hex')
                ->first();
            
            if ($imageWithColor) {
                $colorHex = $imageWithColor->color_hex;
            }
        }
 
        return view('admin.products.images.index', [
            'stock' => $stock,
            'images' => $images,
            'colorHex' => $colorHex,
        ]);
    }

        ]);
    }

    /**
     * Store a newly created image in storage.
     */
    public function store(Request $request, Stock $stock_id)
    {
        // Log all request data for debugging
        Log::info('ProductImageController@store - Request data', [
            'stock_id' => $stock_id->id,
            'all_data' => $request->all(),
            'has_file' => $request->hasFile('images'),
            'files_count' => $request->hasFile('images') ? count($request->file('images')) : 0,
            'has_colors' => $request->has('selected_colors'),
            'has_colors_backup' => $request->has('selected_colors_backup'),
            'has_sizes' => $request->has('sizes'),
            'has_price' => $request->has('variant_price'),
            'has_quantity' => $request->has('stock_quantity'),
        ]);

        // Rename variable to match expected name in views
        $stock = $stock_id;
        $request->validate([
            'images.*' => 'required|image|mimes:jpeg,png,jpg,gif,webp|max:2048',
            'selected_colors' => 'nullable|array',
            'selected_colors.*' => 'nullable|string|regex:/^#[A-Fa-f0-9]{6}$/',
            'sizes' => 'nullable|array',
            'sizes.*' => 'nullable|string|in:XS,S,M,L,XL,XXL',
            'variant_price' => 'nullable|numeric|min:0',
            'stock_quantity' => 'nullable|integer|min:0',
            'color_group' => 'nullable|string|max:100',
        ]);

        try {
            // Prevent duplicate submissions using debug token
            $debugToken = $request->input('debug_token');
            $sessionKey = 'upload_token_'.$stock->id;

            if ($debugToken && session($sessionKey) === $debugToken) {
                Log::info('Duplicate submission detected', ['token' => $debugToken]);

                return redirect()->back()->with('info', 'Upload already in progress or completed.');
            }

            // Store the token to prevent duplicates
            if ($debugToken) {
                session([$sessionKey => $debugToken]);
            }

            DB::beginTransaction();
            Log::info(' begin transaction');

            if (! $request->hasFile('images')) {
                Log::info(' no images uploaded');
                throw new \Exception('No images uploaded');
            }
            Log::info(' has images');

            // Log that we're starting the image upload process
            Log::info('Starting image upload process', [
                'stock_id' => $stock->id,
                'image_count' => count($request->file('images')),
            ]);

            // Store all uploaded images first
            $uploadedImages = [];
            $isPrimarySet = ProductImage::where('stock_id', $stock->id)->exists();

            // Generate a default color group if none provided - same for all images in this batch
            $colorGroup = $request->input('color_group');
            if (empty($colorGroup)) {
                $colorGroup = 'group_'.time();
            }
            Log::info(' color group: '.$colorGroup);

            // Get the color hex value if provided
            $colorHex = $request->filled('selected_colors') ? $request->selected_colors[0] : null;
            Log::info(' color hex: '.$colorHex);

            foreach ($request->file('images') as $index => $image) {
                // Get original filename and extension
                $extension = $image->getClientOriginalExtension();
                $filename = uniqid().'.'.$extension;
                $filePath = 'stocks/'.$filename;
                Log::info(' file path: '.$filePath);
                // Store the image using StorageService
                $uploaded = app(StorageService::class)->putFile(
                    $image,
                    $filePath,
                    [
                        'ContentType' => $image->getMimeType(),
                        'CacheControl' => 'public, max-age=2592000',
                    ]
                );

                if (! $uploaded) {
                    throw new \Exception('Failed to upload image to storage');
                }

                // Create the product image with the correct path
                $productImage = new ProductImage([
                    'image_path' => $filePath,
                    'stock_id' => $stock->id,
                    'sort_order' => ProductImage::where('stock_id', $stock->id)->max('sort_order') + 1,
                    'is_primary' => ! $isPrimarySet && $index === 0, // Make first image primary only if no primary exists
                    'is_group_primary' => $index === 0, // First image in upload batch is group primary by default
                    'color_group' => $colorGroup, // Same color group for all images in this batch
                    'color_hex' => $colorHex, // Same color for all images in this batch
                ]);
                $productImage->save();

                // Set flag after first image is set as primary
                if ($index === 0) {
                    $isPrimarySet = true;
                }

                // Add to uploaded images array
                $uploadedImages[] = $productImage;

                // Log the upload
                $imageUrl = app(StorageService::class)->getUrl($filePath);
                Log::info('Image uploaded successfully', [
                    'stock_id' => $stock->id,
                    'image_path' => $filePath,
                    'url' => $imageUrl,
                ]);
            }

            // Create variants for all images using the same color selections
            if ($request->has('sizes') && $request->has('selected_colors') &&
                $request->has('stock_quantity')) {

                // If no variant price provided, use the product's base price
                if (!$request->filled('variant_price')) {
                    $request->merge(['variant_price' => $stock->current_unit_sale_price]);
                }

exec

    // Methods
    public function getDiscountedPrice()
    {
        if ($this->discount_price && $this->discount_start_date && $this->discount_end_date) {
            $now = Carbon::now();
            $startDate = Carbon::parse($this->discount_start_date);
            $endDate = Carbon::parse($this->discount_end_date);
            if ($now->between($startDate, $endDate)) {
                return $this->discount_price;
            }
        }

        return $this->current_sale_unit_price;
    }

<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Admin;

use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use App\Models\ProductImage;
use App\Models\Stock;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Storage;
use Illuminate\Support\Str;
use Illuminate\Validation\Rule;

class ProductManagementController extends Controller
{
    public function manage(Stock $stock_id)
    {
        $stock = $stock_id->load(['category', 'unit', 'variants', 'variants.images', 'productImages']);

        $categories = \App\Models\Category::orderBy('category_name_en')->get();

        return view('admin.products.manage.index', compact('stock', 'categories'));
    }

    public function index(Request $request)
    {
        $query = Stock::with(['brand', 'category', 'images'])
            ->when($request->search, function ($q) use ($request) {
                return $q->where(function ($query) use ($request) {
                    $query->where('product_name_en', 'like', "%{$request->search}%")
                        ->orWhere('product_name_ar', 'like', "%{$request->search}%")
                        ->orWhere('sku', 'like', "%{$request->search}%");
                });
            })
            ->when($request->category_id, function ($q) use ($request) {
                return $q->where('category_id', $request->category_id);
            })
            ->when($request->brand_id, function ($q) use ($request) {
                return $q->where('brand_id', $request->brand_id);
            })
            ->when($request->status, function ($q) use ($request) {
                return $q->where('status', $request->status);
            });

        $products = $query->paginate($request->per_page ?? 15);

        return response()->json($products);
    }

    public function store(Request $request)
    {
        $request->validate([
            'product_name_en' => 'required|string|max:255',
            'product_name_ar' => 'required|string|max:255',
            'category_id' => 'required|exists:categories,id',
            'brand_id' => 'required|exists:brands,id',
            'sku' => 'required|unique:stocks,sku',
            'description_en' => 'nullable|string',
            'description_ar' => 'nullable|string',
            'current_purchase_unit_price' => 'required|numeric|min:0',
            'current_sale_unit_price' => 'required|numeric|min:0',
            'images.*' => 'nullable|image|max:2048', // Max 2MB per image
            'meta_title' => 'nullable|string|max:255',
            'meta_description' => 'nullable|string',
            'size' => 'nullable|string|max:50',
            'color' => 'nullable|string|max:50',
            'weight' => 'nullable|numeric|min:0',
            'dimensions' => 'nullable|array',
            'dimensions.length' => 'required_with:dimensions|numeric|min:0',
            'dimensions.width' => 'required_with:dimensions|numeric|min:0',
            'dimensions.height' => 'required_with:dimensions|numeric|min:0',
        ]);

        DB::beginTransaction();
        try {
            // Create slug from product name
            $slug = Str::slug($request->product_name_en);

            // Create the product
            $product = Stock::create([
                'product_name_en' => $request->product_name_en,
                'product_name_ar' => $request->product_name_ar,
                'slug' => $slug,
                'category_id' => $request->category_id,
                'brand_id' => $request->brand_id,
                'sku' => $request->sku,
                'description_en' => $request->description_en,
                'description_ar' => $request->description_ar,
                'current_purchase_unit_price' => $request->current_purchase_unit_price,
                'current_sale_unit_price' => $request->current_sale_unit_price,
                'meta_title' => $request->meta_title,
                'meta_description' => $request->meta_description,
                'size' => $request->size,
                'color' => $request->color,
                'weight' => $request->weight,
                'dimensions' => $request->dimensions,
                'status' => 'in_stock',
                'track_inventory' => true,
            ]);

            // Handle image uploads
            if ($request->hasFile('images')) {
                foreach ($request->file('images') as $index => $image) {
                    $path = $image->store('products', 'public');
                    ProductImage::create([
                        'stock_id' => $product->id,
                        'image_path' => $path,
                        'is_primary' => $index === 0,
                        'sort_order' => $index,
                        'alt_text' => $request->product_name_en,
                    ]);
                }
            }

            DB::commit();

            return response()->json($product->load(['images', 'brand', 'category']), 201);
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            DB::rollBack();

            return response()->json(['message' => 'Error creating product', 'error' => $e->getMessage()], 500);
        }
    }

    public function show($id)
    {
        $product = Stock::with(['brand', 'category', 'images', 'reviews.user'])
            ->findOrFail($id);

        return response()->json($product);
    }

    public function update(Request $request, $id)
    {
        $product = Stock::findOrFail($id);

        $request->validate([
            'product_name_en' => 'sometimes|required|string|max:255',
            'product_name_ar' => 'sometimes|required|string|max:255',
            'category_id' => 'sometimes|required|exists:categories,id',
            'brand_id' => 'sometimes|required|exists:brands,id',
            'sku' => ['sometimes', 'required', Rule::unique('stocks')->ignore($id)],
            'description_en' => 'nullable|string',
            'description_ar' => 'nullable|string',
            'current_purchase_unit_price' => 'sometimes|required|numeric|min:0',
            'current_sale_unit_price' => 'sometimes|required|numeric|min:0',
            'new_images.*' => 'nullable|image|max:2048',
            'remove_images.*' => 'nullable|exists:product_images,id',
            'meta_title' => 'nullable|string|max:255',
            'meta_description' => 'nullable|string',
            'size' => 'nullable|string|max:50',
            'color' => 'nullable|string|max:50',
            'weight' => 'nullable|numeric|min:0',
            'dimensions' => 'nullable|array',
            'dimensions.length' => 'required_with:dimensions|numeric|min:0',
            'dimensions.width' => 'required_with:dimensions|numeric|min:0',
            'dimensions.height' => 'required_with:dimensions|numeric|min:0',
        ]);

        DB::beginTransaction();
        try {
            // Update slug if name changed
            if ($request->has('product_name_en')) {
                $request->merge(['slug' => Str::slug($request->product_name_en)]);
            }

            $product->update($request->only([
                'product_name_en', 'product_name_ar', 'slug', 'category_id', 'brand_id', 'sku',
                'description_en', 'description_ar', 'current_purchase_unit_price', 'current_sale_unit_price',
                'meta_title', 'meta_description', 'size', 'color', 'weight', 'dimensions', 'status',
            ]));

            // Handle image removals
            if ($request->has('remove_images')) {
                foreach ($request->remove_images as $imageId) {
                    $image = ProductImage::find($imageId);
                    if ($image && $image->stock_id === $product->id) {
                        Storage::disk('public')->delete($image->image_path);
                        $image->delete();
                    }
                }
            }

            // Handle new image uploads
            if ($request->hasFile('new_images')) {
                $currentMaxOrder = $product->images()->max('sort_order') ?? -1;
                foreach ($request->file('new_images') as $index => $image) {
                    $path = $image->store('products', 'public');
                    ProductImage::create([
                        'stock_id' => $product->id,
                        'image_path' => $path,
                        'is_primary' => false,
                        'sort_order' => $currentMaxOrder + $index + 1,
                        'alt_text' => $product->product_name_en,
                    ]);
                }
            }

            DB::commit();

            return response()->json($product->load(['images', 'brand', 'category']));
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            DB::rollBack();

            return response()->json(['message' => 'Error updating product', 'error' => $e->getMessage()], 500);
        }
    }

    public function destroy($id)
    {
        $product = Stock::findOrFail($id);

        DB::beginTransaction();
        try {
            // Delete associated images from storage
            foreach ($product->images as $image) {
                Storage::disk('public')->delete($image->image_path);
            }

            $product->delete();
            DB::commit();

            return response()->json(['message' => 'Product deleted successfully']);
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            DB::rollBack();

            return response()->json(['message' => 'Error deleting product', 'error' => $e->getMessage()], 500);
        }
    }

    public function updateImages(Request $request, $id)
    {
        $request->validate([
            'images' => 'required|array',
            'images.*.id' => 'required|exists:product_images,id',
            'images.*.is_primary' => 'required|boolean',
            'images.*.sort_order' => 'required|integer|min:0',
            'images.*.alt_text' => 'nullable|string|max:255',
        ]);

        DB::beginTransaction();
        try {
            foreach ($request->images as $imageData) {
                ProductImage::where('id', $imageData['id'])
                    ->where('stock_id', $id)
                    ->update([
                        'is_primary' => $imageData['is_primary'],
                        'sort_order' => $imageData['sort_order'],
                        'alt_text' => $imageData['alt_text'] ?? null,
                    ]);
            }

            DB::commit();

            return response()->json(['message' => 'Images updated successfully']);
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            DB::rollBack();

            return response()->json(['message' => 'Error updating images', 'error' => $e->getMessage()], 500);
        }

<?php

namespace App\Models;

use App\Services\CacheService;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\SoftDeletes;

class ProductVariant extends Model
{
    use SoftDeletes;

    protected $fillable = [
        'stock_id',
        'sku',
        'name',
        'price',
        'quantity',
        'attributes',
        'is_default',
        'is_active',
    ];

    protected $casts = [
        'is_default' => 'boolean',
        'is_active' => 'boolean',
        'price' => 'decimal:2',
        'attributes' => 'json',
    ];

    protected $appends = ['decoded_attributes'];

    /**
     * Get the stock that this variant belongs to
     */
    public function stock()
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Stock::class);
    }

    public function size()
    {
        return $this->belongsToMany(VariantSize::class, 'variant_attribute_values', 'variant_id', 'size_id')
            ->withTimestamps()
            ->latest();
    }

    public function fabric()
    {
        return $this->belongsToMany(VariantFabric::class, 'variant_attribute_values', 'variant_id', 'fabric_id')
            ->withTimestamps()
            ->latest();
    }

    public function color()
    {
        return $this->belongsToMany(VariantColor::class, 'variant_attribute_values', 'variant_id', 'color_id')
            ->withTimestamps()
            ->latest();
    }

    /**
     * Get all images associated with this variant
     */
    public function images()
    {
        return $this->belongsToMany(ProductImage::class, 'variant_images', 'variant_id', 'image_id')
            ->withPivot('is_primary', 'sort_order')
            ->orderBy('sort_order');
    }

    /**
     * Get the primary image for this variant
     */
    public function primaryImage()
    {
        return $this->images()->wherePivot('is_primary', true)->first();
    }

    /**
     * Set the primary image for this variant
     */
    public function setPrimaryImage(ProductImage $image)
    {
        // Remove primary status from all other images
        $this->images()->updateExistingPivot($image->id, ['is_primary' => false]);

        // Set the new primary image
        $this->images()->updateExistingPivot($image->id, ['is_primary' => true]);
    }

    /**
     * Add images to this variant
     */
    public function addImages(array $imageIds, $primaryImageId = null)
    {
        $attachData = [];
        foreach ($imageIds as $index => $imageId) {
            $attachData[$imageId] = [
                'sort_order' => $index,
                'is_primary' => $imageId == $primaryImageId,
            ];
        }

        $this->images()->sync($attachData);
    }

    /**
     * Get the sizes associated with this variant
     */
    public function sizes()
    {
        return $this->belongsToMany(VariantSize::class, 'variant_attribute_values', 'variant_id', 'size_id')
            ->withTimestamps();
    }

    /**
     * Get the colors associated with this variant
     */
    public function colors()
    {
        return $this->belongsToMany(VariantColor::class, 'variant_attribute_values', 'variant_id', 'color_id')
            ->withTimestamps();
    }

    /**
     * Get the fabrics associated with this variant
     */
    public function fabrics()
    {
        return $this->belongsToMany(VariantFabric::class, 'variant_attribute_values', 'variant_id', 'fabric_id')
            ->withTimestamps();
    }

    /**
     * Get the decoded attributes
     *
     * @return array
     */
    public function getDecodedAttributesAttribute()
    {
        if (empty($this->attributes['attributes'])) {
            return [];
        }

        return json_decode($this->attributes['attributes'], true) ?? [];
    }

    /**
     * Get attribute name safely, handling different return types
     *
     * @param  string  $relation  The relation name (size, color, fabric)
     * @param  string  $default  Default value if attribute is not found
     * @return string The attribute name or default value
     */
    public function getAttributeName($relation, $default = '-')
    {
        if (! $this->$relation) {
            return $default;
        }

        // If it's a collection, get the first item
        if ($this->$relation instanceof \Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Collection) {
            $item = $this->$relation->first();
            if (! $item) {
                return $default;
            }

            // Check for translated_name first, then name
            return $item->translated_name ?? $item->name ?? $default;
        }

        // If it's an object with getAttribute method
        if (is_object($this->$relation) && method_exists($this->$relation, 'getAttribute')) {
            return $this->$relation->translated_name ??
                   $this->$relation->getAttribute('name') ??
                   $default;
        }

        // If it's an array with name key
        if (is_array($this->$relation) && isset($this->$relation['name'])) {
            return $this->$relation['name'];
        }

        return $default;
    }

    protected static function boot()
    {
        parent::boot();

        static::saved(function ($variant) {
            app(CacheService::class)->clearBestSellers();
        });

        static::deleted(function ($variant) {
            app(CacheService::class)->clearBestSellers();
        });
    }
}

<?php

namespace App\Models;

use App\Services\StorageService;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\SoftDeletes;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Storage;

class ProductImage extends Model
{
    use SoftDeletes;

    protected $fillable = [
        'stock_id',
        'image_path',
        'is_primary',
        'is_group_primary',
        'color_group',
        'color_hex',
        'view_type',
        'sort_order',
        'alt_text',
    ];

    protected $casts = [
        'sort_order' => 'integer',
    ];

    protected $appends = ['url', 'image_path'];

    /**
     * Get the stock that owns the image.
     */
    public function stock()
    {
        return $this->belongsTo(Stock::class);
    }

    /**
     * Get the variants associated with this image.
     */
    public function variants()
    {
        return $this->belongsToMany(ProductVariant::class, 'variant_images')
            ->withPivot('is_primary', 'sort_order')
            ->withTimestamps();
    }

    /**
     * Get the full URL for the image.
     */
    public function getUrlAttribute()
    {
        if (! $this->image_path) {
            return asset('images/placeholder.png');
        }

        return app(StorageService::class)->getUrl($this->image_path);
    }

    /**
     * Get just the image name without the path
     */
    public function getImageNameAttribute()
    {
        if (! $this->image_path) {
            return 'No image';
        }

        return app(StorageService::class)->getImageNameFromPath($this->image_path);
    }

    /**
     * Set this image as the primary image for a variant
     */
    public function setPrimaryForVariant(ProductVariant $variant)
    {
        // Remove primary status from other images for this variant
        $variant->images()->updateExistingPivot(
            $variant->images()->where('is_primary', true)->pluck('product_images.id'),
            ['is_primary' => false]
        );

        // Set this image as primary
        $variant->images()->updateExistingPivot($this->id, ['is_primary' => true]);
    }

    /**
     * Delete the image file when the model is deleted
     */
    protected static function boot()
    {
        parent::boot();

        static::deleting(function ($image) {
            if ($image->image_path && Storage::exists('public/'.$image->image_path)) {
                Storage::delete('public/'.$image->image_path);
            }
        });
    }

    public function variantImages()
    {
        return $this->hasMany(VariantImage::class);
    }

    /**
     * Get the image path for use in views, returning a default if image is null
     */
    public function getImagePathAttribute()
    {
        if (empty($this->attributes['image_path'])) {
            return 'images/placeholder.png';
        }

        return $this->attributes['image_path'];
    }
}

<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers\API\Frontend;

use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use App\Models\Category;
use App\Models\Stock;
use App\Services\CacheService;

class CategoryProductsController extends Controller
{
    /**
     * Get products for men's category
     *
     * @return \Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse
     */
    public function getMensProducts(Request $request)
    {
        try {
            $locale = $request->input('locale', 'en');
            $cacheKey = 'mens_products_'.$locale;
            // clear cache
            app(CacheService::class)->forget($cacheKey);

            return app(CacheService::class)->remember($cacheKey, function () use ($locale) {
                // Try to find the Men's category
                $category = Category::where('category_name_en', 'Men')
                    ->orWhere('category_name_ar', 'رجال')
                    ->first();

                // Get products from database
                $products = $this->getProductsByCategory($category, $locale);

                return response()->json([
                    'success' => true,
                    'data' => $products,
                    'message' => 'Men products retrieved successfully',
                ]);
            }, 60);

        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            Log::error('Error fetching men\'s products:', [
                'error' => $e->getMessage(),
                'trace' => $e->getTraceAsString(),
            ]);

            return $this->getMockCategoryResponse('men', $locale);
        }
    }
