    /**
     * Get products by category with proper caching and eager loading
     */
    private function getProductsByCategory(Category $category, string $locale): Collection
    {
        // Cache key for this category's products
        $cacheKey = 'category_products_'.$category->id.'_'.$locale;
        Log::info('Cache key for category products:', ['cacheKey' => $cacheKey, 'category_id' => $category->id]);

        // Try to get from cache first but use a shorter cache duration to ensure fresh data
        return app(CacheService::class)->remember($cacheKey, function () use ($category, $locale) {
            // Get all subcategory IDs for this category
            $subcategoryIds = $this->getAllSubcategoryIds($category);

            // Add the main category ID to the list
            $categoryIds = array_merge([$category->id], $subcategoryIds);

            Log::info('Fetching products from categories:', ['category_ids' => $categoryIds]);

            $stocks = Stock::with([
                'variants' => function ($query) {
                    $query->where('is_active', true)
                        ->with(['sizes', 'colors', 'fabrics']);
                },
                'images',
                'reviews',
            ])
                ->select([
                    'id',
                    'product_name_en as name_en',
                    'product_name_ar as name_ar',
                    'description_en',
                    'description_ar',
                    'current_sale_unit_price',
                    'quantity',
                    'is_custom',
                    'is_featured',
                    'category_id',
                    'created_at',
                    'is_active',
                ])
                ->withAvg('reviews', 'rating')
                ->withCount('reviews')
                ->whereIn('category_id', $categoryIds) // Use whereIn to get products from all relevant categories
                ->where('is_active', true)
                ->where('quantity', '>', 0)
                ->orderBy('created_at', 'desc')
                ->take(24) // Increase limit to show more real products
                ->get();

            // Map products with proper localization
            return $stocks->map(function ($stock) use ($locale) {
                $defaultVariant = $stock->variants->first();
                $discountPrice = null;

                if ($defaultVariant && $defaultVariant->discount_price > 0) {
                    $discountPrice = $defaultVariant->discount_price;
                }

                return [
                    'id' => $stock->id,
                    'name' => $locale == 'ar' ? $stock->name_ar : $stock->name_en,
                    'description' => $locale == 'ar' ? $stock->description_ar : $stock->description_en,
                    'price' => $defaultVariant ? $defaultVariant->price : $stock->current_sale_unit_price,
                    'discount_price' => $discountPrice,
                    'main_image' => $stock->images->first() ? ImageService::getContaboUrl($stock->images->first()->image_path ?? $stock->images->first()->path) : null,
                    'images' => $stock->images->map(function ($image) {
                        return ImageService::getContaboUrl($image->image_path ?? $image->path);
                    })->toArray(),
                    'variants' => $stock->variants->map(function ($variant) {
                        return [
                            'id' => $variant->id,
                            'name' => $variant->name,
                            'quantity' => $variant->quantity,
                            'price' => $variant->price,
                            'discount_price' => $variant->discount_price,
                            // Free-text attribute pairs (Size/Color/…) written by seller & admin
                            // variant forms. Storefront falls back to these when the relational
                            // colors/sizes/fabrics pivots are empty. Additive — existing keys kept.
                            'attributes' => $variant->decoded_attributes,
                            'colors' => $variant->colors->map(function ($color) {
                                return [
                                    'id' => $color->id,
                                    'name' => $color->name,
                                    'code' => $color->code,
                                ];
                            }),
                            'sizes' => $variant->sizes->map(function ($size) {
                                return [
                                    'id' => $size->id,
                                    'name' => $size->name,
                                    'code' => $size->code,
                                ];
                            }),
                            'fabrics' => $variant->fabrics->map(function ($fabric) {
                                return [
                                    'id' => $fabric->id,
                                    'name' => $fabric->name,
                                ];
                            }),
                        ];
                    }),
                    'is_custom' => (bool) $stock->is_custom,
                    'is_featured' => (bool) $stock->is_featured,
                    'rating' => $stock->reviews_avg_rating ?? 0,
                    'review_count' => $stock->reviews_count ?? 0,
                    'in_stock' => $stock->quantity > 0,
                ];
            });
        }, 60);
    }

    /**
     * Add stock to all variants with a specific color.
     *
     * @param  string  $color
     * @return \Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse
     */
    public function addColorStock(Request $request, Stock $stock_id, $color)
    {
        // Rename the variable to match the expected name in views
        $stock = $stock_id;

        $request->validate([
            'quantity_to_add' => 'required|integer|min:1',
        ]);

        try {
            // Get the color record
            $colorRecord = VariantColor::where('hex_code', $color)->first();

            if (! $colorRecord) {
                return response()->json([
                    'success' => false,
                    'message' => __('messages.color_not_found'),
                ], 404);
            }

            // Get all variants with this color for this stock
            $variants = ProductVariant::whereHas('color', function ($query) use ($color) {
                $query->where('hex_code', $color);
            })->where('stock_id', $stock->id)
                ->get();

            // Increment quantity for each variant
            foreach ($variants as $variant) {
                $variant->increment('quantity', $request->quantity_to_add);
            }

            // Clear the stock's total quantity cache
            $this->clearStockQuantityCache($stock);

            return response()->json([
                'success' => true,
                'message' => __('messages.stock_added_successfully'),
                'updated_count' => count($variants),
            ]);
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            Log::error('Error adding color stock: '.$e->getMessage());

            return response()->json([
                'success' => false,
                'message' => __('messages.update_failed'),
            ], 500);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Clear the total quantity cache for a stock
     *
     * @return void
     */
    protected function clearStockQuantityCache(Stock $stock)
    {
        $cacheKey = Stock::CACHE_KEY_TOTAL_QUANTITY.$stock->id;
        cache()->forget($cacheKey);
    }
}

    /**
     * Update variant inventory
     */
    public function updateInventory(UpdateVariantInventoryRequest $request, $id)
    {
        $variant = ProductVariant::findOrFail($id);
        $oldQuantity = $variant->quantity;

        DB::beginTransaction();
        try {
            // Update variant quantity
            $variant->update(['quantity' => $request->quantity]);

            // Create inventory history record
            InventoryHistory::create([
                'variant_id' => $variant->id,
                'old_quantity' => $oldQuantity,
                'new_quantity' => $request->quantity,
                'reason' => $request->reason,
                'note' => $request->note,
                'user_id' => auth()->id(),
            ]);

            DB::commit();

            return response()->json([
                'message' => __('Inventory updated successfully'),
                'variant' => $variant->fresh(),
            ]);
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            DB::rollBack();

            return response()->json(['error' => __('Failed to update inventory')], 500);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get inventory history for a variant
     */
    public function getInventoryHistory($id)
    {
        $variant = ProductVariant::findOrFail($id);
        $history = $variant->inventoryHistory()
            ->with('user:id,name')
            ->latest()
            ->paginate(10);

        return response()->json($history);
    }

    public function getProductSelect2(Request $request)
    {
        $search = $request->search;
        $productName = $this->languageService->resolveLocalizedFieldName('product_name');

        return Stock::where('branch_id', Auth::user()->branch_id)
            ->where(function ($query) use ($productName, $search) {
                $query->where($productName, 'like', "%{$search}%")
                    ->orWhere('barcode', 'like', "%{$search}%");
            })
            ->get();
    }

    private function addInitialStock($stock, $invoiceNumber = null)
    {
        $financialYear = FinanceYear::isFinanceYearActive();
        $amount = $stock->quantity * $stock->current_purchase_unit_price;

        $inventorySetting = AccountingService::getAccountSetting(
            AccountHead::ASSETS,
            AccountControl::CURRENT_ASSETS,
            AccountSubControl::INVENTORY,
            AccountActivity::INVENTORY_ADJUSTMENT
        );

        if (! $invoiceNumber) {
            $invoiceNumber = 'INIT'.str_pad($stock->id, 6, '0', STR_PAD_LEFT);
        }

        AccountingService::setEntries(
            $financialYear->id,
            $inventorySetting->account_head_id,
            $inventorySetting->account_control_id,
            $inventorySetting->account_sub_control_id,
            $invoiceNumber,
            now(),
            Auth::id(),
            Auth::user()->branch_id,
            0,
            $amount,
            "Initial stock addition: {$stock->product_name_en}",
            "إضافة المخزون الأولي: {$stock->product_name_ar}"
        );

        $capitalContributionSetting = AccountingService::getAccountSetting(
            AccountHead::EQUITY,
            AccountControl::OWNERS_EQUITY,
            AccountSubControl::CAPITAL_CONTRIBUTION,
            AccountActivity::CAPITAL_CONTRIBUTION
        );

        AccountingService::setEntries(
            $financialYear->id,
            $capitalContributionSetting->account_head_id,
            $capitalContributionSetting->account_control_id,
            $capitalContributionSetting->account_sub_control_id,
            $invoiceNumber,
            now(),
            Auth::id(),
            Auth::user()->branch_id,
            $amount,
            0,
            "Capital contribution for initial stock: {$stock->product_name_en}",
            "مساهمة رأس المال للمخزون الأولي: {$stock->product_name_ar}"
        );
    }

    private function generateImageFilename($image, $productName, $stockId): string
    {
        $extension = $image->getClientOriginalExtension();
        $sanitizedName = Str::slug($productName);

        return "stock_{$stockId}_{$sanitizedName}.{$extension}";
    }

    private function handleImageUpload(Request $request, Stock $stock, string $productName): ?string
    {
        try {
            if (! $request->hasFile('product_image')) {
                return null;
            }

            $file = $request->file('product_image');
            if (! $file->isValid()) {
                throw new \Exception('Invalid file upload');
            }

            // Generate filename
            $filename = $this->generateImageFilename($file, $productName, $stock->id);
            $filePath = 'stocks/'.$filename;

            // Use StorageService to handle the upload with proper credentials
            $uploaded = app(StorageService::class)->putFile(
                $file,
                $filePath,
                [
                    'ContentType' => $file->getMimeType(),
                    'CacheControl' => 'public, max-age=2592000',
                ]
            );

            if (! $uploaded) {
                throw new \Exception('Failed to upload image to storage');
            }

            // Get the URL for logging
            // Get the URL for logging
            $imageUrl = app(StorageService::class)->getUrl($filePath);
            \Log::info('Stock image uploaded successfully', [
                'stock_id' => $stock->id,
                'filename' => $filename,
                'path' => $filePath,
                'url' => $imageUrl,
            ]);

            // Create ProductImage record
            if ($stock->id) {
                ProductImage::create([
                    'stock_id' => $stock->id,
                    'image_path' => $filePath,
                    'is_primary' => true,
                    'sort_order' => ProductImage::where('stock_id', $stock->id)->max('sort_order') + 1,
                ]);
            }

            return $filePath;
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            Log::error('Image upload failed', [
                'error' => $e->getMessage(),
                'stock_id' => $stock->id,
                'product_name' => $productName,
            ]);
            throw $e;
        }
    }

    public function checkAvailability($id, ?Request $request = null)
    {
        try {
            // First try to find the variant by ID
            $variant = ProductVariant::where('id', $id)
                ->where('is_active', true)
                ->first();

            if ($variant) {
                // We found a valid variant
                $availableQuantity = $variant->quantity;
                $stockId = $variant->stock_id;
                $variantId = $variant->id;

                // Check if the variant's stock exists and is active
                $stock = Stock::find($stockId);

                if (! $stock || $stock->status !== 'active') {
                    return response()->json([
                        'available_quantity' => 0,
                        'status' => 'out_of_stock',
                        'stock_id' => $stockId,
                        'variant_id' => $variantId,
                        'success' => true,
                        'message' => 'Product is not available',
                    ], 200);
                }
            } else {

                // No variant found, check if it's a stock ID
                $stock = Stock::with(['variants' => function ($query) {
                    $query->where('is_active', true);
                }])->find($id);
                if (! $stock) {
                    Log::info('Neither stock nor variant found', ['id' => $id]);

                    return response()->json([
                        'available_quantity' => 0,
                        'status' => 'not_found',
                        'message' => 'Product not found',
                        'success' => true,
                    ], 404);
                }

                // Get the total_quantity from the calculated attribute which uses variants
                $availableQuantity = $stock->total_quantity;

                // If no variants exist or total_quantity is 0, fall back to the stock's direct quantity
                if ($availableQuantity <= 0 && $stock->quantity > 0) {
                    $availableQuantity = $stock->quantity;
                    Log::info('Using direct stock quantity as fallback', [
                        'stock_id' => $id,
                        'stock_quantity' => $stock->quantity,
                        'variant_total' => $availableQuantity,
                    ]);
                }

                $stockId = $id;
                $variantId = null;
            }

            // Determine stock status
            $status = 'in_stock';
            if ($availableQuantity <= 0) {
                $status = 'out_of_stock';
            } elseif ($availableQuantity <= 5) { // Threshold for low stock
                $status = 'low_stock';
            }

            // Set stock ID and variant ID for response
            $stockId = $stockId ?? $id;
            $variantId = $variantId ?? null;

            // Cache the result for 5 minutes to reduce database load
            $cacheKey = $variantId
                ? "stock:{$stockId}:variant:{$variantId}:availability"
                : "stock:{$stockId}:availability";

            $cacheData = [
                'available_quantity' => $availableQuantity,
                'status' => $status,
                'stock_id' => $stockId,
                'variant_id' => $variantId,
                'last_checked' => now()->toIso8601String(),
            ];

            Cache::put($cacheKey, $cacheData, now()->addMinutes(5));

            return response()->json([
                'available_quantity' => $availableQuantity,
                'status' => $status,
                'stock_id' => $stockId,
                'variant_id' => $variantId,
                'success' => true,
            ]);

        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            Log::error('Error checking stock availability', [
                'id' => $id,
                'error' => $e->getMessage(),
                'trace' => $e->getTraceAsString(),
            ]);

            return response()->json([
                'available_quantity' => 0,
                'status' => 'error',
                'stock_id' => null,
                'variant_id' => null,
                'success' => false,
                'message' => 'Error checking availability',
            ], 500);
        }
    }

            ->with('success', __('messages.product_saved'));
    }

    /**
     * Soft-delete a product by flipping is_deleted=true (matches existing data convention).
     */
    public function destroy($id)
    {
        $storeOrRedirect = $this->resolveStore();
        if (! $storeOrRedirect instanceof Store) {
            return $storeOrRedirect;
        }
        $store = $storeOrRedirect;

        $product = Stock::where('store_id', $store->id)
            ->where('is_deleted', false)
            ->find($id);

        if (! $product) {
            abort(403);
        }

        // Convention: existing JSON API filters by is_deleted=false; flip to true.
        // (Stock also uses SoftDeletes, but spec is explicit about is_deleted=true only.)
        $product->is_deleted = true;
        $product->is_active = 0;
        $product->save();

        return redirect()->route('seller.products.index')
            ->with('success', __('messages.product_deleted'));
    }
}

    /**
     * Create variants for a product image
     */
    private function createVariants(Request $request, Stock $stock, ProductImage $productImage)
    {
        // Ensure we have a valid price - use stock's current_sale_unit_price as fallback
        $variantPrice = $request->variant_price ?? $stock->current_sale_unit_price;
        
        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Starting variant creation process', [
            'stock_id' => $stock->id,
            'stock_name' => $stock->product_name,
            'sizes' => $request->sizes,
            'selected_colors' => $request->selected_colors,
            'variant_price' => $request->variant_price,
            'effective_price' => $variantPrice,
            'stock_base_price' => $stock->current_sale_unit_price,
            'stock_quantity' => $request->stock_quantity,
            'product_image_id' => $productImage->id,
            'user_id' => auth()->id(),
            'timestamp' => now()->toDateTimeString()
        ]);

        $variantCount = 0;
        $totalCombinations = count($request->sizes) * count($request->selected_colors);

        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Total combinations to create', [
            'total_combinations' => $totalCombinations
        ]);

        foreach ($request->sizes as $size) {
            foreach ($request->selected_colors as $hexColor) {
                $variantCount++;
                
                Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Creating variant combination', [
                    'combination' => "{$variantCount}/{$totalCombinations}",
                    'size' => $size,
                    'hex_color' => $hexColor
                ]);

                    try {

                        // Create or find the attribute values
                        $variantSize = VariantSize::firstOrCreate(['name' => $size]);
                        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Variant size processed', [
                            'size_id' => $variantSize->id,
                            'size_name' => $variantSize->name,
                            'was_created' => $variantSize->wasRecentlyCreated
                        ]);

                        $variantColor = VariantColor::firstOrCreate([
                            'name' => $hexColor,
                            'hex_code' => $hexColor,
                            'description' => 'Extracted from image',
                        ]);
                        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Variant color processed', [
                            'color_id' => $variantColor->id,
                            'color_hex' => $variantColor->hex_code,
                            'was_created' => $variantColor->wasRecentlyCreated
                        ]);



                        // Generate SKU
                        $generatedSku = $this->generateSku($stock, $size, $hexColor);
                        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Generated SKU', [
                            'sku' => $generatedSku
                        ]);

                        // Create the variant
                        $variant = new ProductVariant([
                            'stock_id' => $stock->id,
                            'price' => $variantPrice,
                            'quantity' => $request->stock_quantity,
                            'sku' => $generatedSku,
                            'name' => "{$stock->product_name} - {$size}",
                        ]);
                        
                        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - About to save variant', [
                            'variant_data' => [
                                'stock_id' => $variant->stock_id,
                                'price' => $variant->price,
                                'quantity' => $variant->quantity,
                                'sku' => $variant->sku,
                                'name' => $variant->name
                            ]
                        ]);

                        $variant->save();

                        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Variant saved successfully', [
                            'variant_id' => $variant->id,
                            'variant_sku' => $variant->sku,
                            'variant_name' => $variant->name
                        ]);

                        // Attach attributes to the variant
                        $attributeData = [
                            'variant_id' => $variant->id,
                            'size_id' => $variantSize->id,
                            'color_id' => $variantColor->id,
                            'created_at' => now(),
                            'updated_at' => now(),
                        ];
                        
                        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Inserting variant attributes', [
                            'attribute_data' => $attributeData
                        ]);

                        DB::table('variant_attribute_values')->insert($attributeData);

                        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Variant attributes inserted successfully');

                        // Attach the image to the variant
                        $imageAttachment = [
                            'variant_id' => $variant->id,
                            'image_id' => $productImage->id,
                            'is_primary' => true,
                            'sort_order' => 0,
                            'created_at' => now(),
                            'updated_at' => now(),
                        ];

                        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Inserting image attachment', [
                            'image_attachment' => $imageAttachment
                        ]);

                        DB::table('variant_images')->insert($imageAttachment);

                        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Image attachment inserted successfully', [
                            'variant_id' => $variant->id,
                            'image_id' => $productImage->id
                        ]);

                        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Variant creation completed for combination', [
                            'combination' => "{$variantCount}/{$totalCombinations}",
                            'variant_id' => $variant->id
                        ]);

                    } catch (\Exception $e) {
                        Log::error('ProductImageController::createVariants - Failed to create variant', [
                            'error_message' => $e->getMessage(),
                            'error_file' => $e->getFile(),
                            'error_line' => $e->getLine(),
                            'error_trace' => $e->getTraceAsString(),
                            'combination' => "{$variantCount}/{$totalCombinations}",
                            'size' => $size,
                            'hex_color' => $hexColor,
                            'stock_id' => $stock->id
                        ]);
                        
                        // Continue with next combination instead of failing completely
                        continue;
                    }
                }
        }

        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Variant creation process completed', [
            'total_combinations_processed' => $variantCount,
            'expected_combinations' => $totalCombinations,
            'stock_id' => $stock->id
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * Create variants for a group of product images
     * This creates variants once and associates them with all images in the group
     */
    private function createGroupVariants(Request $request, Stock $stock, array $productImages)
    {
        // Ensure we have a valid price - use stock's current_sale_unit_price as fallback
        $variantPrice = $request->variant_price ?? $stock->current_sale_unit_price;
        
        \Log::info('ProductImageController::createGroupVariants - Starting group variant creation process', [
            'stock_id' => $stock->id,
            'stock_name' => $stock->product_name,
            'sizes' => $request->sizes,
            'selected_colors' => $request->selected_colors,
            'variant_price' => $request->variant_price,
            'effective_price' => $variantPrice,

    public function updateInventory(Request $request, $id)
    {
        $request->validate([
            'min_stock_level' => 'sometimes|required|integer|min:0',
            'max_stock_level' => 'sometimes|required|integer|min:0',
            'track_inventory' => 'sometimes|required|boolean',
            'status' => ['sometimes', 'required', Rule::in(['in_stock', 'out_of_stock', 'discontinued'])],
        ]);

        $product = Stock::findOrFail($id);
        $product->update($request->only(['min_stock_level', 'max_stock_level', 'track_inventory', 'status']));

        return response()->json($product);
    }

    public function updatePricing(Request $request, $id)
    {
        $request->validate([
            'current_purchase_unit_price' => 'sometimes|required|numeric|min:0',
            'current_sale_unit_price' => 'sometimes|required|numeric|min:0',
            'discount_price' => 'nullable|numeric|min:0',
            'discount_start_date' => 'nullable|date|required_with:discount_price',
            'discount_end_date' => 'nullable|date|required_with:discount_price|after:discount_start_date',
        ]);

        $product = Stock::findOrFail($id);
        $product->update($request->only([
            'current_purchase_unit_price', 'current_sale_unit_price',
            'discount_price', 'discount_start_date', 'discount_end_date',
        ]));

        return response()->json($product);
    }
}

    public function relatedProducts()
    {
        return $this->belongsToMany(Stock::class, 'related_products', 'stock_id', 'related_stock_id')
            ->withPivot('relation_type')
            ->withTimestamps();
    }

    public function wishlists(): MorphMany
    {
        return $this->morphMany(CustomerWishlist::class, 'wishlistable');
    }

    // Scopes
    public function scopeActive($query)
    {
        return $query->where('status', 'active');
    }

    public function scopeFeatured($query)
    {
        return $query->where('is_featured', true);
    }

    // Methods
    public function getDiscountedPrice()
    {
        if ($this->discount_price && $this->discount_start_date && $this->discount_end_date) {
            $now = Carbon::now();
            $startDate = Carbon::parse($this->discount_start_date);
            $endDate = Carbon::parse($this->discount_end_date);
            if ($now->between($startDate, $endDate)) {
                return $this->discount_price;
            }
        }

        return $this->current_sale_unit_price;
    }

    public function isInStock()
    {
        return $this->quantity > 0;
    }

    public function isLowStock()
    {
        return $this->quantity <= $this->min_stock_level;
    }

    public function isOverStock()
    {
        return $this->quantity >= $this->max_stock_level;
    }

    /**
     * Get the image URL for the stock.
     */
    public function getImageUrlAttribute()
    {
        try {
            if ($this->relationLoaded('productImages')) {
                $primaryImage = $this->productImages->where('is_primary', true)->first()
                    ?? $this->productImages->first();
            } else {
                $primaryImage = $this->productImages()->where('is_primary', true)->first()
                    ?? $this->productImages()->first();
            }

            if ($primaryImage && $primaryImage->image_path) {
                return app(StorageService::class)->getUrl($primaryImage->image_path);
            }

            // Try product_image if it exists
            if ($this->product_image) {
                return asset('storage/'.$this->product_image);
            }

            // Fallback to direct image if it exists
            if ($this->image) {
                return app(StorageService::class)->getUrl($this->image);
            }
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            \Log::error('Error generating image URL: '.$e->getMessage(), [
                'stock_id' => $this->id,
                'exception' => $e->getTraceAsString(),
            ]);
        }

        // Return a placeholder image if no image was found
        return asset('images/placeholder-product.png');
    }

    /**
     * Get the total quantity of all variants for this stock
     *
     * @return int
     */
    public function getTotalQuantityAttribute()
    {
        try {
            // Use loaded relationship when available to avoid N+1
            if ($this->relationLoaded('variants')) {
                return $this->variants->sum('quantity');
            }

            // Check if we have the value in cache
            $cacheKey = self::CACHE_KEY_TOTAL_QUANTITY.$this->id;

            return \Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache::remember($cacheKey, 300, function () {
                return $this->variants()->sum('quantity');
            });
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            \Log::error('Error calculating total quantity: '.$e->getMessage(), [
                'stock_id' => $this->id,
                'exception' => $e->getTraceAsString(),
            ]);

            return 0;
        }
    }

    /**
     * Get the image name from the image path
     *
     * @return string
     */
    public function getImageNameAttribute()
    {
        try {
            if ($this->relationLoaded('productImages')) {
                $primaryImage = $this->productImages->where('is_primary', true)->first()
                    ?? $this->productImages->first();
            } else {
                $primaryImage = $this->productImages()->where('is_primary', true)->first()
                    ?? $this->productImages()->first();
            }

            if ($primaryImage && $primaryImage->image_path) {
                return app(StorageService::class)->getImageNameFromPath($primaryImage->image_path);
            }

            // Fallback to direct image
            if ($this->image) {
                return app(StorageService::class)->getImageNameFromPath($this->image);
            }
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            \Log::error('Error getting image name: '.$e->getMessage());
        }

        return 'No image';
    }
}

   103	    public function store(Request $request)
   104	    {
   105	        $storeOrRedirect = $this->resolveStore();
   106	        if (! $storeOrRedirect instanceof Store) {
   107	            return $storeOrRedirect;
   108	        }
   109	        $store = $storeOrRedirect;
   110	
   111	        $validated = $request->validate([
   112	            'product_name_en'         => 'required|string|max:255',
   113	            'product_name_ar'         => 'nullable|string|max:255',

   115	            'description_ar'          => 'nullable|string|max:5000',
   116	            'category_id'             => 'required|exists:categories,id',
   117	            'current_sale_unit_price' => 'required|numeric|min:0',
   118	            'quantity'                => 'required|integer|min:0',
   119	            'is_active'               => 'nullable|boolean',
   120	            'product_image'           => 'nullable|image|max:5120', // 5 MB
   121	        ]);
   122	
   123	        try {
   124	            DB::beginTransaction();
   125	
   126	            $stock = new Stock();
   127	            $stock->store_id = $store->id;
   128	            $stock->user_id  = Auth::id();
   129	            $stock->company_id = $store->company_id ?? Auth::user()->company_id ?? null;
   130	            $stock->branch_id  = $store->branch_id ?? Auth::user()->branch_id ?? null;
   131	            $stock->category_id = $validated['category_id'];
   132	            $stock->product_name_en = $validated['product_name_en'];
   133	            $stock->product_name_ar = $validated['product_name_ar'] ?? null;
   134	            $stock->description     = $validated['description'] ?? null;
   135	            $stock->description_ar  = $validated['description_ar'] ?? null;
   136	            $stock->current_sale_unit_price = $validated['current_sale_unit_price'];
   137	            $stock->quantity        = $validated['quantity'];
   138	            $stock->type            = 'Finished Product';
   139	            $stock->slug            = Str::slug($validated['product_name_en']) . '-' . Str::random(6);
   140	            // Direct attribute assignment — is_active/is_deleted live on the table but not in $fillable.
   141	            $stock->is_active  = $request->boolean('is_active', true) ? 1 : 0;
   142	            $stock->is_deleted = false;
   143	
   144	            if ($request->hasFile('product_image')) {
   145	                $file = $request->file('product_image');
   146	                $path = 'stocks/' . $store->id . '/' . time() . '_' . Str::random(8) . '.' . $file->getClientOriginalExtension();
   147	                $stored = app(StorageService::class)->putFile($file, $path);
   148	                if ($stored !== false) {
   149	                    $stock->image = $path;
   150	                }
   151	            }
   152	
   153	            $stock->save();
   154	
   155	            DB::commit();
   156	        } catch (\Throwable $e) {
   157	            DB::rollBack();
   158	            Log::error('Seller\\ProductController::store failed', [
   159	                'store_id' => $store->id,
   160	                'error'    => $e->getMessage(),
   161	            ]);
   162	
   163	            return back()->withInput()->with('error', __('messages.something_went_wrong'));
   164	        }
   165	
   166	        return redirect()->route('seller.products.show', $stock->id)
   167	            ->with('success', __('messages.product_saved'));
   168	    }

   247	        ]);

   255	            $product->description            = $validated['description'] ?? $product->description;
   256	            $product->description_ar         = $validated['description_ar'] ?? $product->description_ar;
   257	            $product->current_sale_unit_price = $validated['current_sale_unit_price'];
   258	            $product->quantity               = $validated['quantity'];
   259	            $product->is_active              = $request->boolean('is_active', (bool) $product->is_active) ? 1 : 0;
   260	
   261	            if ($request->hasFile('product_image')) {
   262	                $file = $request->file('product_image');
   263	                $path = 'stocks/' . $store->id . '/' . time() . '_' . Str::random(8) . '.' . $file->getClientOriginalExtension();
   264	                $stored = app(StorageService::class)->putFile($file, $path);

   288	    /**
   289	     * Soft-delete a product by flipping is_deleted=true (matches existing data convention).
   290	     */
   291	    public function destroy($id)
   292	    {
   293	        $storeOrRedirect = $this->resolveStore();
   294	        if (! $storeOrRedirect instanceof Store) {
   295	            return $storeOrRedirect;
   296	        }
   297	        $store = $storeOrRedirect;
   298	
   299	        $product = Stock::where('store_id', $store->id)
   300	            ->where('is_deleted', false)
   301	            ->find($id);
   302	
   303	        if (! $product) {
   304	            abort(403);
   305	        }
   306	
   307	        // Convention: existing JSON API filters by is_deleted=false; flip to true.
   308	        // (Stock also uses SoftDeletes, but spec is explicit about is_deleted=true only.)
   309	        $product->is_deleted = true;
   310	        $product->is_active = 0;
   311	        $product->save();
   312	
   313	        return redirect()->route('seller.products.index')
   314	            ->with('success', __('messages.product_deleted'));
   315	    }

   244	    // Methods
   245	    public function getDiscountedPrice()
   246	    {
   247	        if ($this->discount_price && $this->discount_start_date && $this->discount_end_date) {
   248	            $now = Carbon::now();
   249	            $startDate = Carbon::parse($this->discount_start_date);
   250	            $endDate = Carbon::parse($this->discount_end_date);
   251	            if ($now->between($startDate, $endDate)) {
   252	                return $this->discount_price;
   253	            }
   254	        }
   255	
   256	        return $this->current_sale_unit_price;
   257	    }

   274	    /**
   275	     * Get the image URL for the stock.
   276	     */
   277	    public function getImageUrlAttribute()
   278	    {
   279	        try {
   280	            if ($this->relationLoaded('productImages')) {
   281	                $primaryImage = $this->productImages->where('is_primary', true)->first()
   282	                    ?? $this->productImages->first();
   283	            } else {
   284	                $primaryImage = $this->productImages()->where('is_primary', true)->first()
   285	                    ?? $this->productImages()->first();
   286	            }
   287	
   288	            if ($primaryImage && $primaryImage->image_path) {
   289	                return app(StorageService::class)->getUrl($primaryImage->image_path);
   290	            }
   291	
   292	            // Try product_image if it exists
   293	            if ($this->product_image) {
   294	                return asset('storage/'.$this->product_image);
   295	            }
   296	
   297	            // Fallback to direct image if it exists
   298	            if ($this->image) {
   299	                return app(StorageService::class)->getUrl($this->image);
   300	            }
   301	        } catch (\Exception $e) {
   302	            \Log::error('Error generating image URL: '.$e->getMessage(), [
   303	                'stock_id' => $this->id,
   304	                'exception' => $e->getTraceAsString(),
   305	            ]);
   306	        }
   307	
   308	        // Return a placeholder image if no image was found
   309	        return asset('images/placeholder-product.png');
   310	    }
   311	
   312	    /**
   313	     * Get the total quantity of all variants for this stock
   314	     *
   315	     * @return int
   316	     */
   317	    public function getTotalQuantityAttribute()
   318	    {
   319	        try {
   320	            // Use loaded relationship when available to avoid N+1
   321	            if ($this->relationLoaded('variants')) {
   322	                return $this->variants->sum('quantity');
   323	            }
   324	
   325	            // Check if we have the value in cache
   326	            $cacheKey = self::CACHE_KEY_TOTAL_QUANTITY.$this->id;
   327	
   328	            return \Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache::remember($cacheKey, 300, function () {
   329	                return $this->variants()->sum('quantity');
   330	            });
   331	        } catch (\Exception $e) {
   332	            \Log::error('Error calculating total quantity: '.$e->getMessage(), [
   333	                'stock_id' => $this->id,
   334	                'exception' => $e->getTraceAsString(),
   335	            ]);
   336	
   337	            return 0;
   338	        }
   339	    }
   340	
   341	    /**
   342	     * Get the image name from the image path
   343	     *
   344	     * @return string
   345	     */
   346	    public function getImageNameAttribute()
   347	    {
   348	        try {
   349	            if ($this->relationLoaded('productImages')) {
   350	                $primaryImage = $this->productImages->where('is_primary', true)->first()
   351	                    ?? $this->productImages->first();
   352	            } else {
   353	                $primaryImage = $this->productImages()->where('is_primary', true)->first()
   354	                    ?? $this->productImages()->first();
   355	            }
   356	
   357	            if ($primaryImage && $primaryImage->image_path) {
   358	                return app(StorageService::class)->getImageNameFromPath($primaryImage->image_path);
   359	            }
   360	
   361	            // Fallback to direct image
   362	            if ($this->image) {
   363	                return app(StorageService::class)->getImageNameFromPath($this->image);
   364	            }
   365	        } catch (\Exception $e) {
   366	            \Log::error('Error getting image name: '.$e->getMessage());
   367	        }
   368	
   369	        return 'No image';
   370	    }

   130	    /**
   131	     * Get products by category with proper caching and eager loading
   132	     */
   133	    private function getProductsByCategory(Category $category, string $locale): Collection
   134	    {
   135	        // Cache key for this category's products
   136	        $cacheKey = 'category_products_'.$category->id.'_'.$locale;
   137	        Log::info('Cache key for category products:', ['cacheKey' => $cacheKey, 'category_id' => $category->id]);
   138	
   139	        // Try to get from cache first but use a shorter cache duration to ensure fresh data
   140	        return app(CacheService::class)->remember($cacheKey, function () use ($category, $locale) {
   141	            // Get all subcategory IDs for this category
   142	            $subcategoryIds = $this->getAllSubcategoryIds($category);
   143	
   144	            // Add the main category ID to the list
   145	            $categoryIds = array_merge([$category->id], $subcategoryIds);
   146	
   147	            Log::info('Fetching products from categories:', ['category_ids' => $categoryIds]);
   148	
   149	            $stocks = Stock::with([
   150	                'variants' => function ($query) {
   151	                    $query->where('is_active', true)
   152	                        ->with(['sizes', 'colors', 'fabrics']);
   153	                },
   154	                'images',
   155	                'reviews',
   156	            ])
   157	                ->select([
   158	                    'id',
   159	                    'product_name_en as name_en',
   160	                    'product_name_ar as name_ar',
   161	                    'description_en',
   162	                    'description_ar',
   163	                    'current_sale_unit_price',
   164	                    'quantity',
   165	                    'is_custom',
   166	                    'is_featured',
   167	                    'category_id',
   168	                    'created_at',
   169	                    'is_active',
   170	                ])
   171	                ->withAvg('reviews', 'rating')
   172	                ->withCount('reviews')
   173	                ->whereIn('category_id', $categoryIds) // Use whereIn to get products from all relevant categories
   174	                ->where('is_active', true)
   175	                ->where('quantity', '>', 0)
   176	                ->orderBy('created_at', 'desc')
   177	                ->take(24) // Increase limit to show more real products
   178	                ->get();
   179	
   180	            // Map products with proper localization
   181	            return $stocks->map(function ($stock) use ($locale) {
   182	                $defaultVariant = $stock->variants->first();
   183	                $discountPrice = null;
   184	
   185	                if ($defaultVariant && $defaultVariant->discount_price > 0) {
   186	                    $discountPrice = $defaultVariant->discount_price;
   187	                }
   188	
   189	                return [
   190	                    'id' => $stock->id,
   191	                    'name' => $locale == 'ar' ? $stock->name_ar : $stock->name_en,
   192	                    'description' => $locale == 'ar' ? $stock->description_ar : $stock->description_en,
   193	                    'price' => $defaultVariant ? $defaultVariant->price : $stock->current_sale_unit_price,
   194	                    'discount_price' => $discountPrice,
   195	                    'main_image' => $stock->images->first() ? ImageService::getContaboUrl($stock->images->first()->image_path ?? $stock->images->first()->path) : null,
   196	                    'images' => $stock->images->map(function ($image) {
   197	                        return ImageService::getContaboUrl($image->image_path ?? $image->path);
   198	                    })->toArray(),
   199	                    'variants' => $stock->variants->map(function ($variant) {
   200	                        return [
   201	                            'id' => $variant->id,
   202	                            'name' => $variant->name,
   203	                            'quantity' => $variant->quantity,
   204	                            'price' => $variant->price,
   205	                            'discount_price' => $variant->discount_price,
   206	                            // Free-text attribute pairs (Size/Color/…) written by seller & admin
   207	                            // variant forms. Storefront falls back to these when the relational
   208	                            // colors/sizes/fabrics pivots are empty. Additive — existing keys kept.
   209	                            'attributes' => $variant->decoded_attributes,
   210	                            'colors' => $variant->colors->map(function ($color) {
   211	                                return [
   212	                                    'id' => $color->id,
   213	                                    'name' => $color->name,
   214	                                    'code' => $color->code,
   215	                                ];
   216	                            }),
   217	                            'sizes' => $variant->sizes->map(function ($size) {
   218	                                return [
   219	                                    'id' => $size->id,
   220	                                    'name' => $size->name,
   221	                                    'code' => $size->code,
   222	                                ];
   223	                            }),

   228	                                ];
   229	                            }),
   230	                        ];
   231	                    }),
   232	                    'is_custom' => (bool) $stock->is_custom,
   233	                    'is_featured' => (bool) $stock->is_featured,
   234	                    'rating' => $stock->reviews_avg_rating ?? 0,
   235	                    'review_count' => $stock->reviews_count ?? 0,
   236	                    'in_stock' => $stock->quantity > 0,

    44	            ->withTimestamps()
    45	            ->latest();
    46	    }

    52	            ->latest();
    53	    }

    59	            ->latest();
    60	    }

    63	     * Get all images associated with this variant

    65	    public function images()
    66	    {

    78	    }

    83	    public function setPrimaryImage(ProductImage $image)
    84	    {
    85	        // Remove primary status from all other images
    86	        $this->images()->updateExistingPivot($image->id, ['is_primary' => false]);
    87	
    88	        // Set the new primary image
    89	        $this->images()->updateExistingPivot($image->id, ['is_primary' => true]);
    90	    }

    93	     * Add images to this variant
    94	     */
    95	    public function addImages(array $imageIds, $primaryImageId = null)
    96	    {
    97	        $attachData = [];
    98	        foreach ($imageIds as $index => $imageId) {
    99	            $attachData[$imageId] = [
   100	                'sort_order' => $index,
   101	                'is_primary' => $imageId == $primaryImageId,
   102	            ];
   103	        }
   104	
   105	        $this->images()->sync($attachData);
   106	    }

   132	            ->withTimestamps();

   134	
   135	    /**
   136	     * Get the decoded attributes
   137	     *
   138	     * @return array
   139	     */
   140	    public function getDecodedAttributesAttribute()
   141	    {
   142	        if (empty($this->attributes['attributes'])) {
   143	            return [];
   144	        }
   145	
   146	        return json_decode($this->attributes['attributes'], true) ?? [];
   147	    }
   148	
   149	    /**
   150	     * Get attribute name safely, handling different return types
   151	     *
   152	     * @param  string  $relation  The relation name (size, color, fabric)
   153	     * @param  string  $default  Default value if attribute is not found
   154	     * @return string The attribute name or default value
   155	     */
   156	    public function getAttributeName($relation, $default = '-')
   157	    {
   158	        if (! $this->$relation) {
   159	            return $default;
   160	        }
   161	
   162	        // If it's a collection, get the first item
   163	        if ($this->$relation instanceof \Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Collection) {
   164	            $item = $this->$relation->first();
   165	            if (! $item) {
   166	                return $default;
   167	            }
   168	
   169	            // Check for translated_name first, then name
   170	            return $item->translated_name ?? $item->name ?? $default;
   171	        }
   172	
   173	        // If it's an object with getAttribute method
   174	        if (is_object($this->$relation) && method_exists($this->$relation, 'getAttribute')) {
   175	            return $this->$relation->translated_name ??
   176	                   $this->$relation->getAttribute('name') ??
   177	                   $default;
   178	        }
   179	
   180	        // If it's an array with name key
   181	        if (is_array($this->$relation) && isset($this->$relation['name'])) {
   182	            return $this->$relation['name'];
   183	        }
   184	
   185	        return $default;
   186	    }
   187	
   188	    protected static function boot()
   189	    {
   190	        parent::boot();
   191	
   192	        static::saved(function ($variant) {
   193	            app(CacheService::class)->clearBestSellers();
   194	        });
   195	
   196	        static::deleted(function ($variant) {
   197	            app(CacheService::class)->clearBestSellers();
   198	        });
   199	    }

   133	    public function update(Request $request, $id)
   134	    {
   135	        $product = Stock::findOrFail($id);
   136	
   137	        $request->validate([
   138	            'product_name_en' => 'sometimes|required|string|max:255',
   139	            'product_name_ar' => 'sometimes|required|string|max:255',
   140	            'category_id' => 'sometimes|required|exists:categories,id',
   141	            'brand_id' => 'sometimes|required|exists:brands,id',
   142	            'sku' => ['sometimes', 'required', Rule::unique('stocks')->ignore($id)],
   143	            'description_en' => 'nullable|string',
   144	            'description_ar' => 'nullable|string',
   145	            'current_purchase_unit_price' => 'sometimes|required|numeric|min:0',
   146	            'current_sale_unit_price' => 'sometimes|required|numeric|min:0',
   147	            'new_images.*' => 'nullable|image|max:2048',
   148	            'remove_images.*' => 'nullable|exists:product_images,id',
   149	            'meta_title' => 'nullable|string|max:255',
   150	            'meta_description' => 'nullable|string',
   151	            'size' => 'nullable|string|max:50',
   152	            'color' => 'nullable|string|max:50',
   153	            'weight' => 'nullable|numeric|min:0',
   154	            'dimensions' => 'nullable|array',
   155	            'dimensions.length' => 'required_with:dimensions|numeric|min:0',
   156	            'dimensions.width' => 'required_with:dimensions|numeric|min:0',
   157	            'dimensions.height' => 'required_with:dimensions|numeric|min:0',
   158	        ]);
   159	
   160	        DB::beginTransaction();
   161	        try {
   162	            // Update slug if name changed
   163	            if ($request->has('product_name_en')) {
   164	                $request->merge(['slug' => Str::slug($request->product_name_en)]);
   165	            }
   166	
   167	            $product->update($request->only([
   168	                'product_name_en', 'product_name_ar', 'slug', 'category_id', 'brand_id', 'sku',
   169	                'description_en', 'description_ar', 'current_purchase_unit_price', 'current_sale_unit_price',
   170	                'meta_title', 'meta_description', 'size', 'color', 'weight', 'dimensions', 'status',
   171	            ]));
   172	
   173	            // Handle image removals
   174	            if ($request->has('remove_images')) {
   175	                foreach ($request->remove_images as $imageId) {
   176	                    $image = ProductImage::find($imageId);
   177	                    if ($image && $image->stock_id === $product->id) {
   178	                        Storage::disk('public')->delete($image->image_path);
   179	                        $image->delete();
   180	                    }
   181	                }
   182	            }
   183	
   184	            // Handle new image uploads
   185	            if ($request->hasFile('new_images')) {
   186	                $currentMaxOrder = $product->images()->max('sort_order') ?? -1;
   187	                foreach ($request->file('new_images') as $index => $image) {
   188	                    $path = $image->store('products', 'public');
   189	                    ProductImage::create([
   190	                        'stock_id' => $product->id,
   191	                        'image_path' => $path,
   192	                        'is_primary' => false,
   193	                        'sort_order' => $currentMaxOrder + $index + 1,
   194	                        'alt_text' => $product->product_name_en,
   195	                    ]);
   196	                }
   197	            }
   198	
   199	            DB::commit();
   200	
   201	            return response()->json($product->load(['images', 'brand', 'category']));
   202	        } catch (\Exception $e) {
   203	            DB::rollBack();
   204	
   205	            return response()->json(['message' => 'Error updating product', 'error' => $e->getMessage()], 500);
   206	        }
   207	    }

   209	    public function destroy($id)
   210	    {
   211	        $product = Stock::findOrFail($id);
   212	
   213	        DB::beginTransaction();
   214	        try {
   215	            // Delete associated images from storage
   216	            foreach ($product->images as $image) {
   217	                Storage::disk('public')->delete($image->image_path);
   218	            }
   219	
   220	            $product->delete();
   221	            DB::commit();
   222	
   223	            return response()->json(['message' => 'Product deleted successfully']);
   224	        } catch (\Exception $e) {
   225	            DB::rollBack();
   226	
   227	            return response()->json(['message' => 'Error deleting product', 'error' => $e->getMessage()], 500);
   228	        }
   229	    }

   249	                        'alt_text' => $imageData['alt_text'] ?? null,
   250	                    ]);
   251	            }

   256	        } catch (\Exception $e) {

   258

    59	    public function index(Request $request)

    61	
    62	        $productName = $this->languageService->resolveLocalizedFieldName('product_name');
    63	        $authUser = Auth::user();
    64	        if ($authUser->roles[0]->name == 'super-admin') {

    74	                    'is_deleted' => 0,
    75	                ]);

    79

    84	
    85	        // Apply date filter
    86	        if ($request->filled('dateFilter')) {
    87	            $stocks = $this->dateFilter->applyDateFilter($stocks, $request->dateFilter, 'created_at');
    88	        }
    89	
    90	        // Apply pagination
    91	        $stocks = $stocks->latest()->paginate(10);
    92

   148	            $stock->allowtax = $request->allowtax == 1 ? 1 : 0;
   149	
   150	            $stock->is_active = 1;
   151	
   152	            // Save stock first to get ID
   153	            $stock->save();
   154	
   155	            // Handle image upload
   156	            if ($request->hasFile('product_image')) {
   157	                $image = Image::make($request->file('product_image'))
   158	                    ->resize(1200, null, function ($constraint) {
   159	                        $constraint->aspectRatio();
   160	                        $constraint->upsize();
   161	                    });
   162	
   163	                // Only encode as webp if supported
   164	                if (function_exists('imagewebp')) {
   165	                    $image->encode('webp', config('app.image_quality', 75));
   166	                } else {
   167	                    $image->encode('jpg', config('app.image_quality', 75));
   168	                }
   169	
   170	                $stock->image = $this->handleImageUpload($request, $stock, $request->$productName);
   171	            }
   172	
   173	            $this->addInitialStock($stock);
   174	
   175	            DB::commit();
   176	
   177	            // Trigger Next.js revalidation
   178	            $category = Category::find($stock->category_id);
   179	            $this->revalidationService->revalidateProduct($stock->id, $category->slug ?? null);
   180	
   181	            Log::info('Stock created successfully', [
   182	                'stock_id' => $stock->id,
   183	                'image_path' => $stock->image ?? 'no_image',
   184	            ]);
   185	
   186	            Session::flash('message', __('messages.stock_added_successfully'));
   187	
   188	            // Check if this is an AJAX request for inline confirmation
   189	            if ($request->expectsJson() || $request->ajax()) {
   190	                return response()->json([
   191	                    'success' => true,
   192	                    'message' => __('messages.stock_created_successfully'),
   193	                    'stock' => [
   194	                        'id' => $stock->id,
   195	                        'product_name' => $stock->product_name_en ?? $stock->product_name_ar,
   196	                    ],
   197	                    'redirect_url' => 'https://pro.beldify.com/en/admin/products/' . $stock->id . '/images',
   198	                    'stocks_url' => url('stocks')
   199	                ]);
   200	            }
   201	
   202	            // Fallback to redirect for non-AJAX requests
   203	            return redirect()->route('stocks.upload-confirmation', ['id' => $stock->id]);
   204	        } catch (\Exception $e) {
   205	            DB::rollBack();
   206	            Log::error('Stock creation failed: '.$e->getMessage(), [
   207	                'exception' => $e,
   208	                'request_data' => $request->except(['product_image']),
   209	            ]);
   210	            Session::flash('error', __('messages.stock_creation_failed'));
   211	
   212	            return redirect()->back()->withInput();
   213	        }
   214	    }

   237	    public function show($id)

   240

   242	        $variantsByColor = $stock->variants->groupBy(function ($variant) {

   244

   254	    public function update(Request $request, $id)
   255	    {
   256	        $productName = $this->languageService->resolveLocalizedFieldName('product_name');
   257	        $description = $this->languageService->resolveLocalizedFieldName('description');
   258	        $request->validate([
   259	            'category_id' => 'required',
   260	            $productName => 'required',
   261	            $description => 'required',
   262	            'quantity' => 'required',
   263	            'current_sale_unit_price' => 'required',
   264	            'current_purchase_unit_price' => 'required',
   265	            // "type" => "required",
   266	            'image' => 'nullable|image|mimes:jpeg,png,jpg,gif|max:2048',
   267	        ]);
   268	
   269	        $stock = Stock::find($id);
   270	        $oldStock = $stock->toArray();
   271	        $stock->company_id = Auth::user()->company_id;
   272	        $stock->branch_id = Auth::user()->branch_id;
   273	        $stock->user_id = Auth::user()->id;
   274	        $stock->category_id = $request->category_id;
   275	        $stock->$productName = $request->$productName;
   276	        $stock->type = $request->type;
   277	        $stock->$description = $request->$description;
   278	        $stock->quantity = $request->quantity;
   279	        $stock->barcode = $request->barcode;
   280	        $stock->current_sale_unit_price = $request->current_sale_unit_price;
   281	        $stock->current_purchase_unit_price = $request->current_purchase_unit_price;
   282	        $stock->allowtax = $request->allowtax == 1 ? 1 : 0;
   283	        if ($request->hasFile('product_image')) {
   284	            $stock->image = $this->handleImageUpload($request, $stock, $request->$productName);
   285	        }
   286	
   287	        $stock->update();
   288	
   289	        $newStock = $stock->fresh()->toArray();
   290	        Log::info('Stock updated', [
   291	            'user_id' => Auth::id(),
   292	            'stock_id' => $id,
   293	            'old_data' => $oldStock,
   294	            'new_data' => $newStock,
   295	        ]);
   296	
   297	        Session::flash('message', __('messages.stock_updated_successfully'));
   298	
   299	        if ($request->filled('redirect_to') && str_starts_with($request->input('redirect_to'), url('/'))) {
   300	            return redirect($request->input('redirect_to'));
   301	        }
   302	
   303	        return redirect('stocks');
   304	    }

   315	    public function getProductSelect2(Request $request)
   316	    {
   317	        $search = $request->search;
   318	        $productName = $this->languageService->resolveLocalizedFieldName('product_name');
   319	
   320	        return Stock::where('branch_id', Auth::user()->branch_id)
   321	            ->where(function ($query) use ($productName, $search) {
   322	                $query->where($productName, 'like', "%{$search}%")
   323	                    ->orWhere('barcode', 'like', "%{$search}%");

   328	    private function addInitialStock($stock, $invoiceNumber = null)
   329	    {
   330	        $financialYear = FinanceYear::isFinanceYearActive();
   331	        $amount = $stock->quantity * $stock->current_purchase_unit_price;
   332	
   333	        $inventorySetting = AccountingService::getAccountSetting(
   334	            AccountHead::ASSETS,
   335	            AccountControl::CURRENT_ASSETS,
   336	            AccountSubControl::INVENTORY,
   337	            AccountActivity::INVENTORY_ADJUSTMENT
   338	        );
   339	
   340	        if (! $invoiceNumber) {
   341	            $invoiceNumber = 'INIT'.str_pad($stock->id, 6, '0', STR_PAD_LEFT);
   342	        }
   343	
   344	        AccountingService::setEntries(
   345	            $financialYear->id,
   346	            $inventorySetting->account_head_id,
   347	            $inventorySetting->account_control_id,
   348	            $inventorySetting->account_sub_control_id,
   349	            $invoiceNumber,
   350	            now(),
   351	            Auth::id(),
   352	            Auth::user()->branch_id,
   353	            0,
   354	            $amount,
   355	            "Initial stock addition: {$stock->product_name_en}",
   356	            "إضافة المخزون الأولي: {$stock->product_name_ar}"
   357	        );
   358	
   359	        $capitalContributionSetting = AccountingService::getAccountSetting(
   360	            AccountHead::EQUITY,
   361	            AccountControl::OWNERS_EQUITY,
   362	            AccountSubControl::CAPITAL_CONTRIBUTION,
   363	            AccountActivity::CAPITAL_CONTRIBUTION
   364	        );
   365	
   366	        AccountingService::setEntries(
   367	            $financialYear->id,
   368	            $capitalContributionSetting->account_head_id,
   369	            $capitalContributionSetting->account_control_id,
   370	            $capitalContributionSetting->account_sub_control_id,
   371	            $invoiceNumber,
   372	            now(),
   373	            Auth::id(),
   374	            Auth::user()->branch_id,
   375	            $amount,
   376	            0,
   377	            "Capital contribution for initial stock: {$stock->product_name_en}",
   378	            "مساهمة رأس المال للمخزون الأولي: {$stock->product_name_ar}"
   379	        );
   380	    }
   381	
   382	    private function generateImageFilename($image, $productName, $stockId): string
   383	    {
   384	        $extension = $image->getClientOriginalExtension();
   385	        $sanitizedName = Str::slug($productName);
   386	
   387	        return "stock_{$stockId}_{$sanitizedName}.{$extension}";
   388	    }
   389	
   390	    private function handleImageUpload(Request $request, Stock $stock, string $productName): ?string
   391	    {
   392	        try {
   393	            if (! $request->hasFile('product_image')) {
   394	                return null;
   395	            }
   396	
   397	            $file = $request->file('product_image');
   398	            if (! $file->isValid()) {
   399	                throw new \Exception('Invalid file upload');
   400	            }
   401	
   402	            // Generate filename
   403	            $filename = $this->generateImageFilename($file, $productName, $stock->id);
   404	            $filePath = 'stocks/'.$filename;
   405	
   406	            // Use StorageService to handle the upload with proper credentials
   407	            $uploaded = app(StorageService::class)->putFile(
   408	                $file,
   409	                $filePath,
   410	                [
   411	                    'ContentType' => $file->getMimeType(),
   412	                    'CacheControl' => 'public, max-age=2592000',
   413	                ]
   414	            );
   415	
   416	            if (! $uploaded) {
   417	                throw new \Exception('Failed to upload image to storage');
   418	            }
   419	
   420	            // Get the URL for logging

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	<?php
     2	
     3	namespace App\Http\Controllers\Admin;
     4	
     5	use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
     6	use App\Models\ProductVariant;
     7	use App\Models\Stock;
     8	use App\Models\VariantColor;
     9	use Illuminate\Http\Request;
    10	use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
    11	use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;
    12	
    13	class VariantInventoryController extends Controller
    14	{
    15	    /**
    16	     * Display the inventory management page for a product.
    17	     *
    18	     * @param  Stock  $stock_id  The stock model (auto-resolved by Laravel)
    19	     * @return \Illuminate\View\View
    20	     */
    21	    public function index(Stock $stock_id)
    22	    {
    23	        // Rename the variable to match the expected name in views
    24	        $stock = $stock_id;
    25	
    26	        // Get all product images with their color groups
    27	        $productImages = DB::table('product_images')
    28	            ->where('stock_id', $stock->id)
    29	            ->whereNotNull('color_group')
    30	            ->select('color_group', 'color_hex')
    31	            ->distinct()
    32	            ->get()
    33	            ->map(function ($item) {
    34	                // Convert to array to avoid collection property access issues
    35	                return (array) $item;
    36	            });
    37	
    38	        // Get all variants for this stock with optimized eager loading
    39	        $variants = ProductVariant::where('stock_id', $stock->id)
    40	            ->with(['size', 'color', 'fabric', 'images'])
    41	            ->orderBy('created_at', 'desc')
    42	            ->get();
    43	
    44	        // Get primary images for each color group
    45	        $primaryGroupImages = DB::table('product_color_groups')
    46	            ->where('stock_id', $stock->id)
    47	            ->pluck('primary_image_id', 'color_group')
    48	            ->toArray();
    49	
    50	        // Get all product images
    51	        $allImages = DB::table('product_images')
    52	            ->where('stock_id', $stock->id)
    53	            ->get()
    54	            ->keyBy('id');
    55	
    56	        // Create color groups based on product images
    57	        $imageColorGroups = collect();
    58	        foreach ($productImages as $group) {
    59	            $colorGroup = $group['color_group'] ?? null;
    60	            if (! $colorGroup) {
    61	                continue;
    62	            }
    63	
    64	            $imageColorGroups[$colorGroup] = [
    65	                'name' => $colorGroup,
    66	                'color_hex' => $group['color_hex'] ?? null,
    67	                'variants' => collect(),
    68	                'primary_image_id' => $primaryGroupImages[$colorGroup] ?? null,
    69	                'primary_image' => isset($primaryGroupImages[$colorGroup]) ? $allImages[$primaryGroupImages[$colorGroup]] : null,
    70	            ];
    71	        }
    72	
    73	        // Assign variants to image color groups based on their associated images
    74	        foreach ($variants as $variant) {
    75	            $assigned = false;
    76	
    77	            // Check if variant has images and assign to matching color group
    78	            if ($variant->images && $variant->images->isNotEmpty()) {
    79	                foreach ($variant->images as $image) {
    80	                    if (! empty($image->color_group) && isset($imageColorGroups[$image->color_group])) {
    81	                        $imageColorGroups[$image->color_group]['variants']->push($variant);
    82	                        $assigned = true;
    83	                        break;
    84	                    }
    85	                }
    86	            }
    87	
    88	            // If no match with images, try to match by color
    89	            if (! $assigned && $variant->color) {
    90	                // Make sure variant color has a hex_code property before attempting to match
    91	                $variantHexCode = null;
    92	
    93	                // Check if color is an object with hex_code property
    94	                if (is_object($variant->color) && property_exists($variant->color, 'hex_code')) {
    95	                    $variantHexCode = $variant->color->hex_code;
    96	                }
    97	                // If color is an array, check for hex_code key
    98	                elseif (is_array($variant->color) && isset($variant->color['hex_code'])) {
    99	                    $variantHexCode = $variant->color['hex_code'];
   100	                }
   101	
   102	                // Only proceed with matching if we have a valid hex code
   103	                if ($variantHexCode) {
   104	                    foreach ($imageColorGroups as $groupName => $group) {
   105	                        // Make sure group has a valid color_hex value before comparing
   106	                        if (isset($group['color_hex']) && ! empty($group['color_hex']) && $group['color_hex'] == $variantHexCode) {
   107	                            $imageColorGroups[$groupName]['variants']->push($variant);
   108	                            $assigned = true;
   109	                            break;
   110	                        }
   111	                    }
   112	                }
   113	            }
   114	
   115	            // If still no match, add to ungrouped
   116	            if (! $assigned) {
   117	                if (! isset($imageColorGroups['ungrouped'])) {
   118	                    $imageColorGroups['ungrouped'] = [
   119	                        'name' => 'Ungrouped',
   120	                        'color_hex' => null,
   121	                        'variants' => collect(),
   122	                        'primary_image_id' => null,
   123	                        'primary_image' => null,
   124	                    ];
   125	                }
   126	                $imageColorGroups['ungrouped']['variants']->push($variant);
   127	            }
   128	        }
   129	
   130	        // Get unique colors used by this product
   131	        $colors = VariantColor::whereHas('variants', function ($query) use ($stock) {
   132	            $query->where('stock_id', $stock->id);
   133	        })->get();
   134	
   135	        return view('admin.products.inventory.index', [
   136	            'stock' => $stock,
   137	            'variants' => $variants,
   138	            'colorGroups' => $imageColorGroups,
   139	            'colors' => $colors,
   140	        ]);
   141	    }

   143	    /**
   144	     * Update inventory for a specific variant.
   145	     *
   146	     * @param  int  $variant_id
   147	     * @return \Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse
   148	     */
   149	    public function updateInventory(Request $request, $variant_id)
   150	    {
   151	        $request->validate([
   152	            'quantity' => 'required|integer|min:0',
   153	            'price' => 'required|numeric|min:0',
   154	        ]);
   155	
   156	        try {
   157	            $variant = ProductVariant::findOrFail($variant_id);
   158	            $stock = $variant->stock;
   159	
   160	            $variant->update([
   161	                'price' => $request->input('price'),
   162	                'quantity' => $request->input('quantity'),
   163	            ]);
   164	
   165	            // Clear the stock's total quantity cache
   166	            $this->clearStockQuantityCache($stock);
   167	
   168	            return response()->json([
   169	                'success' => true,
   170	                'message' => __('messages.inventory_updated'),
   171	                'variant' => $variant,
   172	            ]);
   173	        } catch (\Exception $e) {
   174	            Log::error('Error updating variant inventory: '.$e->getMessage());
   175	
   176	            return response()->json([
   177	                'success' => false,
   178	                'message' => __('messages.update_failed'),
   179	            ], 500);
   180	        }
   181	    }

   183	    /**
   184	     * Bulk update inventory for multiple variants.
   185	     *
   186	     * @return \Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse
   187	     */
   188	    public function bulkUpdate(Request $request, Stock $stock_id)
   189	    {
   190	        // Rename the variable to match the expected name in views
   191	        $stock = $stock_id;
   192	
   193	        $request->validate([
   194	            'variants' => 'required|array',
   195	            'variants.*.id' => 'required|exists:product_variants,id',
   196	            'variants.*.quantity' => 'required|integer|min:0',
   197	            'variants.*.price' => 'required|numeric|min:0',
   198	        ]);
   199	
   200	        try {
   201	            DB::beginTransaction();
   202	
   203	            foreach ($request->variants as $variantData) {
   204	                ProductVariant::where('id', $variantData['id'])
   205	                    ->update([
   206	                        'quantity' => $variantData['quantity'],
   207	                        'price' => $variantData['price'],
   208	                    ]);
   209	            }
   210	
   211	            DB::commit();
   212	
   213	            // Clear the stock's total quantity cache
   214	            $this->clearStockQuantityCache($stock);
   215	
   216	            return response()->json([
   217	                'success' => true,
   218	                'message' => __('messages.inventory_bulk_updated'),
   219	            ]);
   220	        } catch (\Exception $e) {
   221	            DB::rollBack();
   222	            Log::error('Error bulk updating inventory: '.$e->getMessage());
   223	
   224	            return response()->json([
   225	                'success' => false,
   226	                'message' => __('messages.update_failed'),
   227	            ], 500);
   228	        }
   229	    }

   232	     * Update inventory for all variants with a specific color.

   234	     * @param  string  $color
