   236	     */
   237	    public function updateColorInventory(Request $request, Stock $stock_id, $color)
   238	    {
   239	        // Rename the variable to match the expected name in views
   240	        $stock = $stock_id;
   241	
   242	        $request->validate([
   243	            'quantity' => 'required|integer|min:0',
   244	            'price' => 'required|numeric|min:0',
   245	        ]);
   246	
   247	        try {
   248	            // Get the color record
   249	            $colorRecord = VariantColor::where('hex_code', $color)->first();
   250	
   251	            if (! $colorRecord) {
   252	                return response()->json([
   253	                    'success' => false,
   254	                    'message' => __('messages.color_not_found'),
   255	                ], 404);
   256	            }
   257	
   258	            // Update all variants with this color for this stock
   259	            $variants = ProductVariant::whereHas('color', function ($query) use ($color) {
   260	                $query->where('hex_code', $color);
   261	            })->where('stock_id', $stock->id)
   262	                ->update([
   263	                    'quantity' => $request->quantity,
   264	                    'price' => $request->price,
   265	                ]);
   266	
   267	            // Clear the stock's total quantity cache
   268	            $this->clearStockQuantityCache($stock);
   269	
   270	            return response()->json([
   271	                'success' => true,
   272	                'message' => __('messages.color_inventory_updated'),
   273	                'updated_count' => $variants,
   274	            ]);
   275	        } catch (\Exception $e) {
   276	            Log::error('Error updating color inventory: '.$e->getMessage());
   277	
   278	            return response()->json([
   279	                'success' => false,
   280	                'message' => __('messages.update_failed'),
   281	            ], 500);
   282	        }
   283	    }

   291	    public function addColorStock(Request $request, Stock $stock_id, $color)
   292	    {
   293	        // Rename the variable to match the expected name in views
   294	        $stock = $stock_id;
   295	
   296	        $request->validate([
   297	            'quantity_to_add' => 'required|integer|min:1',
   298	        ]);

   309	            }
   310

   315	                ->get();
   316

   330	        } catch (\Exception $e) {

   332

   340	    /**
   341	     * Clear the total quantity cache for a stock
   342	     *
   343	     * @return void
   344	     */
   345	    protected function clearStockQuantityCache(Stock $stock)
   346	    {

    26	    public function index($stock_id)
    27	    {
    28	        $stock = Stock::findOrFail($stock_id);
    29	
    30	        // Get variants with their relationships
    31	        $variants = ProductVariant::where('stock_id', $stock_id)
    32	            ->with(['size', 'fabric', 'color'])
    33	            ->get()
    34	            ->groupBy(function ($variant) {
    35	                // Group by base SKU (remove the size/color/fabric codes)
    36	                return preg_replace('/-[^-]+-[^-]+-[^-]+$/', '', $variant->sku);
    37	            })
    38	            ->map(function ($groupedVariants) {
    39	                $firstVariant = $groupedVariants->first();
    40	                // Get base name by removing the attribute parts
    41	                $firstVariant->base_name = preg_replace('/\s*-\s*[^-]+\s*-\s*[^-]+$/', '', $firstVariant->name);
    42	                $firstVariant->total_quantity = $groupedVariants->sum('quantity');
    43	                $firstVariant->all_sizes = $groupedVariants->pluck('size')->flatten()->unique('id')->filter();
    44	                $firstVariant->all_fabrics = $groupedVariants->pluck('fabric')->flatten()->unique('id')->filter();
    45	                $firstVariant->all_colors = $groupedVariants->pluck('color')->flatten()->unique('id')->filter();
    46	                $firstVariant->grouped_variants = $groupedVariants;
    47	
    48	                return $firstVariant;
    49	            })
    50	            ->values();
    51	
    52	        return view('admin.variants.index', compact('variants', 'stock'));
    53	    }

    64	    public function store(Request $request, $stock_id)
    65	    {
    66	        $validated = $request->validate([
    67	            'name' => 'required|string|max:255',
    68	            'sku' => 'required|string|unique:product_variants,sku',
    69	            'price' => 'required|numeric|min:0',
    70	            'quantity' => 'required|integer|min:0',
    71	            'attribute_keys' => 'nullable|array',
    72	            'attribute_values' => 'nullable|array',
    73	            'is_default' => 'boolean',
    74	            'is_active' => 'boolean',
    75	        ]);
    76	
    77	        $stock = Stock::findOrFail($stock_id);
    78	
    79	        // Combine attribute keys and values into an associative array
    80	        $attributes = [];
    81	        if (! empty($validated['attribute_keys']) && ! empty($validated['attribute_values'])) {
    82	            foreach ($validated['attribute_keys'] as $index => $key) {
    83	                if (! empty($key) && ! empty($validated['attribute_values'][$index])) {
    84	                    $attributes[$key] = $validated['attribute_values'][$index];
    85	                }
    86	            }
    87	        }
    88	
    89	        // Remove the separate attribute arrays and add the combined attributes
    90	        unset($validated['attribute_keys'], $validated['attribute_values']);
    91	        $validated['attributes'] = json_encode($attributes);
    92	
    93	        $variant = new ProductVariant($validated);
    94	        $variant->stock_id = $stock_id;
    95	        $variant->save();
    96	
    97	        // Attach sizes, fabrics, and colors to the variant using their IDs
    98	        if ($request->has('sizes')) {
    99	            $variant->sizes()->attach($request->input('sizes'));
   100	        }
   101	        if ($request->has('fabrics')) {
   102	            $variant->fabrics()->attach($request->input('fabrics'));
   103	        }
   104	        if ($request->has('selected_colors')) {
   105	            $variant->colors()->attach($request->input('selected_colors'));
   106	        }
   107	
   108	        Session::flash('message', __('Variant added successfully'));
   109	
   110	        if ($request->filled('redirect_to') && str_starts_with($request->input('redirect_to'), url('/'))) {
   111	            return redirect($request->input('redirect_to'));
   112	        }
   113	
   114	        return redirect()->route('admin.variants.index', $stock_id);
   115	    }
   116	
   117	    public function edit($stock_id, $variant_id)

   120	        $stock = Stock::findOrFail($stock_id);
   121	        $variant = ProductVariant::with(['size', 'fabric', 'color'])->findOrFail($variant_id);

   131	    public function update(Request $request, $stock_id, $variant_id)
   132	    {
   133	        $validated = $request->validate([
   134	            'sku' => 'required|string|unique:product_variants,sku,'.$variant_id,
   135	            'price' => 'required|numeric|min:0',
   136	            'quantity' => 'required|integer|min:0',
   137	            'size_id' => 'required|exists:variant_sizes,id',
   138	            'fabric_id' => 'required|exists:variant_fabrics,id',
   139	            'color_id' => 'required|exists:variant_colors,id',
   140	            'is_default' => 'boolean',
   141	            'is_active' => 'boolean',
   142	        ]);
   143	
   144	        DB::beginTransaction();
   145	        try {
   146	            $variant = ProductVariant::findOrFail($variant_id);
   147	            $oldData = $variant->toArray();
   148	
   149	            // Update basic variant information
   150	            $variant->update([
   151	                'sku' => $validated['sku'],
   152	                'price' => $validated['price'],
   153	                'quantity' => $validated['quantity'],
   154	                'is_default' => $request->has('is_default'),
   155	                'is_active' => $request->has('is_active'),
   156	            ]);
   157	
   158	            // If this variant is set as default, remove default status from other variants
   159	            if ($request->has('is_default')) {
   160	                ProductVariant::where('stock_id', $stock_id)
   161	                    ->where('id', '!=', $variant->id)
   162	                    ->update(['is_default' => false]);
   163	            }
   164	
   165	            // Update variant attributes
   166	            DB::table('variant_attribute_values')->updateOrInsert(
   167	                ['variant_id' => $variant->id],
   168	                [
   169	                    'size_id' => $validated['size_id'],
   170	                    'fabric_id' => $validated['fabric_id'],
   171	                    'color_id' => $validated['color_id'],
   172	                    'updated_at' => now(),
   173	                ]
   174	            );
   175	
   176	            // Update variant name based on attributes
   177	            $size = DB::table('variant_sizes')->where('id', $validated['size_id'])->first();
   178	            $fabric = DB::table('variant_fabrics')->where('id', $validated['fabric_id'])->first();
   179	            $color = DB::table('variant_colors')->where('id', $validated['color_id'])->first();
   180	
   181	            $variantName = sprintf(
   182	                '%s - %s - %s - %s',
   183	                $variant->stock->product_name,
   184	                $size->name,
   185	                $fabric->name,
   186	                $color->name
   187	            );
   188	
   189	            $variant->update(['name' => $variantName]);
   190	
   191	            // Log the update
   192	            \Log::info('Variant updated', [
   193	                'variant_id' => $variant->id,
   194	                'old_data' => $oldData,
   195	                'new_data' => array_merge(
   196	                    $variant->fresh()->toArray(),
   197	                    [
   198	                        'size_id' => $validated['size_id'],
   199	                        'fabric_id' => $validated['fabric_id'],
   200	                        'color_id' => $validated['color_id'],
   201	                        'is_active' => $request->has('is_active'),
   202	                        'is_default' => $request->has('is_default'),
   203	                    ]
   204	                ),
   205	            ]);
   206	
   207	            DB::commit();
   208	            Session::flash('message', __('messages.variant_updated_successfully'));
   209	
   210	            if ($request->filled('redirect_to') && str_starts_with($request->input('redirect_to'), url('/'))) {
   211	                return redirect($request->input('redirect_to'));
   212	            }
   213	
   214	            return redirect()->route('admin.variants.index', $stock_id);
   215	
   216	        } catch (\Exception $e) {
   217	            DB::rollback();
   218	            \Log::error('Failed to update variant: '.$e->getMessage(), [
   219	                'variant_id' => $variant_id,
   220	                'error' => $e,
   221	                'request_data' => $request->all(),
   222	            ]);
   223	
   224	            Session::flash('error', __('messages.failed_to_update_variant'));
   225	
   226	            return back()->withInput();
   227	        }
   228	    }

   254	
   255	    /**
   256	     * Handle bulk actions on variants
   257	     */
   258	    public function bulkAction(BulkVariantRequest $request)
   259	    {
   260	        $action = $request->input('action');
   261	        $variantIds = $request->input('variants');
   262	
   263	        DB::beginTransaction();
   264	        try {
   265	            switch ($action) {
   266	                case 'delete':
   267	                    ProductVariant::whereIn('id', $variantIds)->delete();
   268	                    $message = __('Selected variants have been deleted');
   269	                    break;
   270	
   271	                case 'activate':
   272	                    ProductVariant::whereIn('id', $variantIds)->update(['is_active' => true]);
   273	                    $message = __('Selected variants have been activated');
   274	                    break;
   275	
   276	                case 'deactivate':
   277	                    ProductVariant::whereIn('id', $variantIds)->update(['is_active' => false]);
   278	                    $message = __('Selected variants have been deactivated');
   279	                    break;
   280	            }
   281	
   282	            DB::commit();
   283	
   284	            return response()->json(['message' => $message]);
   285	        } catch (\Exception $e) {
   286	            DB::rollBack();
   287	
   288	            return response()->json(['error' => __('Failed to process bulk action')], 500);
   289	        }
   290	    }
   291	
   292	    /**
   293	     * Update variant inventory
   294	     */
   295	    public function updateInventory(UpdateVariantInventoryRequest $request, $id)
   296	    {
   297	        $variant = ProductVariant::findOrFail($id);
   298	        $oldQuantity = $variant->quantity;
   299	
   300	        DB::beginTransaction();
   301	        try {
   302	            // Update variant quantity
   303	            $variant->update(['quantity' => $request->quantity]);
   304	
   305	            // Create inventory history record
   306	            InventoryHistory::create([
   307	                'variant_id' => $variant->id,
   308	                'old_quantity' => $oldQuantity,
   309	                'new_quantity' => $request->quantity,
   310	                'reason' => $request->reason,
   311	                'note' => $request->note,
   312	                'user_id' => auth()->id(),
   313	            ]);
   314	
   315	            DB::commit();
   316	
   317	            return response()->json([
   318	                'message' => __('Inventory updated successfully'),
   319	                'variant' => $variant->fresh(),
   320	            ]);
   321	        } catch (\Exception $e) {
   322	            DB::rollBack();
   323	
   324	            return response()->json(['error' => __('Failed to update inventory')], 500);
   325	        }
   326	    }
   327	
   328	    /**
   329	     * Get inventory history for a variant
   330	     */
   331	    public function getInventoryHistory($id)
   332	    {
   333	        $variant = ProductVariant::findOrFail($id);
   334	        $history = $variant->inventoryHistory()
   335	            ->with('user:id,name')
   336	            ->latest()
   337	            ->paginate(10);
   338	
   339	        return response()->json($history);
   340	    }
   341	}

     1	<?php
     2	
     3	namespace App\Models;
     4	
     5	use App\Services\StorageService;
     6	use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
     7	use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\SoftDeletes;
     8	use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Storage;
     9	
    10	class ProductImage extends Model
    11	{
    12	    use SoftDeletes;
    13	
    14	    protected $fillable = [
    15	        'stock_id',
    16	        'image_path',
    17	        'is_primary',
    18	        'is_group_primary',
    19	        'color_group',
    20	        'color_hex',
    21	        'view_type',
    22	        'sort_order',
    23	        'alt_text',
    24	    ];
    25	
    26	    protected $casts = [
    27	        'sort_order' => 'integer',
    28	    ];
    29	
    30	    protected $appends = ['url', 'image_path'];
    31	
    32	    /**
    33	     * Get the stock that owns the image.
    34	     */
    35	    public function stock()
    36	    {
    37	        return $this->belongsTo(Stock::class);
    38	    }
    39	
    40	    /**
    41	     * Get the variants associated with this image.
    42	     */
    43	    public function variants()
    44	    {
    45	        return $this->belongsToMany(ProductVariant::class, 'variant_images')
    46	            ->withPivot('is_primary', 'sort_order')
    47	            ->withTimestamps();
    48	    }
    49	
    50	    /**
    51	     * Get the full URL for the image.
    52	     */
    53	    public function getUrlAttribute()
    54	    {
    55	        if (! $this->image_path) {
    56	            return asset('images/placeholder.png');
    57	        }
    58	
    59	        return app(StorageService::class)->getUrl($this->image_path);
    60	    }
    61	
    62	    /**
    63	     * Get just the image name without the path
    64	     */
    65	    public function getImageNameAttribute()
    66	    {
    67	        if (! $this->image_path) {
    68	            return 'No image';
    69	        }
    70	
    71	        return app(StorageService::class)->getImageNameFromPath($this->image_path);
    72	    }
    73	
    74	    /**
    75	     * Set this image as the primary image for a variant
    76	     */
    77	    public function setPrimaryForVariant(ProductVariant $variant)
    78	    {
    79	        // Remove primary status from other images for this variant
    80	        $variant->images()->updateExistingPivot(
    81	            $variant->images()->where('is_primary', true)->pluck('product_images.id'),
    82	            ['is_primary' => false]
    83	        );
    84	
    85	        // Set this image as primary
    86	        $variant->images()->updateExistingPivot($this->id, ['is_primary' => true]);
    87	    }
    88	
    89	    /**
    90	     * Delete the image file when the model is deleted
    91	     */
    92	    protected static function boot()
    93	    {
    94	        parent::boot();
    95	
    96	        static::deleting(function ($image) {
    97	            if ($image->image_path && Storage::exists('public/'.$image->image_path)) {
    98	                Storage::delete('public/'.$image->image_path);
    99	            }
   100	        });
   101	    }
   102	
   103	    public function variantImages()
   104	    {
   105	        return $this->hasMany(VariantImage::class);
   106	    }
   107	
   108	    /**
   109	     * Get the image path for use in views, returning a default if image is null
   110	     */
   111	    public function getImagePathAttribute()
   112	    {
   113	        if (empty($this->attributes['image_path'])) {
   114	            return 'images/placeholder.png';
   115	        }
   116	
   117	        return $this->attributes['image_path'];
   118	    }
   119	}

    22	    /**
    23	     * Display a listing of the product images.
    24	     */
    25	    public function index(Request $request, Stock $stock_id)
    26	    {
    27	        // Rename variable to match expected name in views
    28	        $stock = $stock_id;
    29	        $images = collect();
    30	
    31	        // Get images from product_images table
    32	        $query = $stock->images()
    33	            ->orderBy('is_primary', 'desc')
    34	            ->orderBy('sort_order');
    35	
    36	        // If user is not admin, only show images they own
    37	        /** @var User|null $user */
    38	        $user = auth()->user();
    39	        if ($user && ! $user->hasRole('admin') && ! $user->hasRole('super-admin')) {
    40	            // Only show images for products owned by the current user
    41	            if ($stock->user_id != auth()->id()) {
    42	                $query->where('user_id', auth()->id());
    43	            }
    44	        }
    45	
    46	        $productImages = $query->get();
    47	
    48	        if ($productImages->isNotEmpty()) {
    49	            $images = $productImages;
    50	        } elseif ($stock->image) {
    51	            // If no product images but stock has legacy image, create a virtual image object
    52	            $images->push((object) [
    53	                'id' => 0,
    54	                'image_path' => (strpos($stock->image, 'http') === 0) ? $stock->image : 'stocks/'.$stock->image,
    55	                'is_primary' => true,
    56	                'alt_text' => $stock->product_name_en,
    57	                'sort_order' => 0,
    58	            ]);
    59	        }
    60	
    61	        // Get color hex value if color_group parameter is provided
    62	        $colorHex = null;
    63	        if ($request->has('color_group')) {
    64	            $colorGroup = $request->get('color_group');
    65	            // Find the color hex from product images with this color group
    66	            $imageWithColor = ProductImage::where('stock_id', $stock->id)
    67	                ->where('color_group', $colorGroup)
    68	                ->whereNotNull('color_hex')
    69	                ->first();
    70	            
    71	            if ($imageWithColor) {
    72	                $colorHex = $imageWithColor->color_hex;
    73	            }
    74	        }
    75	 
    76	        return view('admin.products.images.index', [
    77	            'stock' => $stock,
    78	            'images' => $images,
    79	            'colorHex' => $colorHex,
    80	        ]);
    81	    }

   127	    /**
   128	     * Store a newly created image in storage.
   129	     */
   130	    public function store(Request $request, Stock $stock_id)
   131	    {
   132	        // Log all request data for debugging
   133	        Log::info('ProductImageController@store - Request data', [
   134	            'stock_id' => $stock_id->id,
   135	            'all_data' => $request->all(),
   136	            'has_file' => $request->hasFile('images'),
   137	            'files_count' => $request->hasFile('images') ? count($request->file('images')) : 0,
   138	            'has_colors' => $request->has('selected_colors'),
   139	            'has_colors_backup' => $request->has('selected_colors_backup'),
   140	            'has_sizes' => $request->has('sizes'),
   141	            'has_price' => $request->has('variant_price'),
   142	            'has_quantity' => $request->has('stock_quantity'),
   143	        ]);
   144	
   145	        // Rename variable to match expected name in views
   146	        $stock = $stock_id;
   147	        $request->validate([
   148	            'images.*' => 'required|image|mimes:jpeg,png,jpg,gif,webp|max:2048',
   149	            'selected_colors' => 'nullable|array',
   150	            'selected_colors.*' => 'nullable|string|regex:/^#[A-Fa-f0-9]{6}$/',
   151	            'sizes' => 'nullable|array',
   152	            'sizes.*' => 'nullable|string|in:XS,S,M,L,XL,XXL',
   153	            'variant_price' => 'nullable|numeric|min:0',
   154	            'stock_quantity' => 'nullable|integer|min:0',
   155	            'color_group' => 'nullable|string|max:100',
   156	        ]);
   157	
   158	        try {
   159	            // Prevent duplicate submissions using debug token
   160	            $debugToken = $request->input('debug_token');
   161	            $sessionKey = 'upload_token_'.$stock->id;
   162	
   163	            if ($debugToken && session($sessionKey) === $debugToken) {
   164	                Log::info('Duplicate submission detected', ['token' => $debugToken]);
   165	
   166	                return redirect()->back()->with('info', 'Upload already in progress or completed.');
   167	            }
   168	
   169	            // Store the token to prevent duplicates
   170	            if ($debugToken) {
   171	                session([$sessionKey => $debugToken]);
   172	            }
   173	
   174	            DB::beginTransaction();
   175	            Log::info(' begin transaction');
   176	
   177	            if (! $request->hasFile('images')) {
   178	                Log::info(' no images uploaded');
   179	                throw new \Exception('No images uploaded');
   180	            }
   181	            Log::info(' has images');
   182	
   183	            // Log that we're starting the image upload process
   184	            Log::info('Starting image upload process', [
   185	                'stock_id' => $stock->id,
   186	                'image_count' => count($request->file('images')),
   187	            ]);
   188	
   189	            // Store all uploaded images first
   190	            $uploadedImages = [];
   191	            $isPrimarySet = ProductImage::where('stock_id', $stock->id)->exists();
   192	
   193	            // Generate a default color group if none provided - same for all images in this batch
   194	            $colorGroup = $request->input('color_group');
   195	            if (empty($colorGroup)) {
   196	                $colorGroup = 'group_'.time();
   197	            }
   198	            Log::info(' color group: '.$colorGroup);
   199	
   200	            // Get the color hex value if provided
   201	            $colorHex = $request->filled('selected_colors') ? $request->selected_colors[0] : null;
   202	            Log::info(' color hex: '.$colorHex);
   203	
   204	            foreach ($request->file('images') as $index => $image) {
   205	                // Get original filename and extension
   206	                $extension = $image->getClientOriginalExtension();
   207	                $filename = uniqid().'.'.$extension;
   208	                $filePath = 'stocks/'.$filename;
   209	                Log::info(' file path: '.$filePath);
   210	                // Store the image using StorageService
   211	                $uploaded = app(StorageService::class)->putFile(
   212	                    $image,
   213	                    $filePath,
   214	                    [
   215	                        'ContentType' => $image->getMimeType(),
   216	                        'CacheControl' => 'public, max-age=2592000',
   217	                    ]
   218	                );
   219	
   220	                if (! $uploaded) {
   221	                    throw new \Exception('Failed to upload image to storage');
   222	                }
   223	
   224	                // Create the product image with the correct path
   225	                $productImage = new ProductImage([
   226	                    'image_path' => $filePath,
   227	                    'stock_id' => $stock->id,
   228	                    'sort_order' => ProductImage::where('stock_id', $stock->id)->max('sort_order') + 1,
   229	                    'is_primary' => ! $isPrimarySet && $index === 0, // Make first image primary only if no primary exists
   230	                    'is_group_primary' => $index === 0, // First image in upload batch is group primary by default
   231	                    'color_group' => $colorGroup, // Same color group for all images in this batch
   232	                    'color_hex' => $colorHex, // Same color for all images in this batch
   233	                ]);
   234	                $productImage->save();
   235	
   236	                // Set flag after first image is set as primary
   237	                if ($index === 0) {
   238	                    $isPrimarySet = true;
   239	                }
   240	
   241	                // Add to uploaded images array
   242	                $uploadedImages[] = $productImage;
   243	
   244	                // Log the upload
   245	                $imageUrl = app(StorageService::class)->getUrl($filePath);
   246	                Log::info('Image uploaded successfully', [
   247	                    'stock_id' => $stock->id,
   248	                    'image_path' => $filePath,
   249	                    'url' => $imageUrl,
   250	                ]);
   251	            }
   252	
   253	            // Create variants for all images using the same color selections
   254	            if ($request->has('sizes') && $request->has('selected_colors') &&
   255	                $request->has('stock_quantity')) {
   256	
   257	                // If no variant price provided, use the product's base price
   258	                if (!$request->filled('variant_price')) {
   259	                    $request->merge(['variant_price' => $stock->current_unit_sale_price]);
   260	                }
   261	
   262	                Log::info('Creating variants with parameters', [
   263	                    'sizes' => $request->sizes,
   264	                    'colors' => $request->selected_colors,
   265	                    'price' => $request->variant_price || $stock->current_unit_sale_price,
   266	                    'quantity' => $request->stock_quantity,
   267	                ]);
   268	
   269	                // Create variants once and associate with all images
   270	                try {
   271	                    $createdVariants = $this->createGroupVariants($request, $stock, $uploadedImages);
   272	
   273	                    Log::info('Created variants for image group', [
   274	                        'stock_id' => $stock->id,
   275	                        'image_count' => count($uploadedImages),
   276	                        'variant_count' => count($createdVariants),
   277	                    ]);
   278	                } catch (\Exception $variantException) {
   279	                    Log::error('Error creating variants: '.$variantException->getMessage(), [
   280	                        'stock_id' => $stock->id,
   281	                        'trace' => $variantException->getTraceAsString(),
   282	                    ]);
   283	                    // Continue with the upload even if variant creation fails
   284	                }
   285	            } else {
   286	                Log::info('Skipping variant creation - missing required fields', [
   287	                    'has_sizes' => $request->has('sizes'),
   288	                    'has_colors' => $request->has('selected_colors'),
   289	                    'has_quantity' => $request->has('stock_quantity'),
   290	                    'note' => 'Price will use product base price if not provided.'
   291	                ]);
   292	            }
   293	
   294	            DB::commit();
   295	
   296	            // Clear the upload token after successful upload
   297	            if ($debugToken) {
   298	                session()->forget($sessionKey);
   299	            }
   300	
   301	            if ($request->filled('redirect_to') && str_starts_with($request->input('redirect_to'), url('/'))) {
   302	                return redirect($request->input('redirect_to'))->with('success', __('messages.images_uploaded_successfully'));
   303	            }
   304	
   305	            return redirect()->back()->with('success', __('messages.images_uploaded_successfully'));
   306	        } catch (\Exception $e) {
   307	            DB::rollBack();
   308	            Log::error('Error uploading images: '.$e->getMessage(), [
   309	                'stock_id' => $stock->id,
   310	                'request_data' => $request->except(['images']),
   311	                'trace' => $e->getTraceAsString(),
   312	                'file' => $e->getFile(),
   313	                'line' => $e->getLine(),
   314	            ]);
   315	
   316	            return redirect()->back()->with('error', __('messages.failed_to_upload_images').': '.$e->getMessage());
   317	        }
   318	    }

   320	    /**
   321	     * Create variants for a product image
   322	     */
   323	    private function createVariants(Request $request, Stock $stock, ProductImage $productImage)
   324	    {
   325	        // Ensure we have a valid price - use stock's current_sale_unit_price as fallback
   326	        $variantPrice = $request->variant_price ?? $stock->current_sale_unit_price;
   327	        
   328	        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Starting variant creation process', [
   329	            'stock_id' => $stock->id,
   330	            'stock_name' => $stock->product_name,
   331	            'sizes' => $request->sizes,
   332	            'selected_colors' => $request->selected_colors,
   333	            'variant_price' => $request->variant_price,
   334	            'effective_price' => $variantPrice,
   335	            'stock_base_price' => $stock->current_sale_unit_price,
   336	            'stock_quantity' => $request->stock_quantity,
   337	            'product_image_id' => $productImage->id,
   338	            'user_id' => auth()->id(),
   339	            'timestamp' => now()->toDateTimeString()
   340	        ]);
   341	
   342	        $variantCount = 0;
   343	        $totalCombinations = count($request->sizes) * count($request->selected_colors);
   344	
   345	        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Total combinations to create', [
   346	            'total_combinations' => $totalCombinations
   347	        ]);
   348	
   349	        foreach ($request->sizes as $size) {
   350	            foreach ($request->selected_colors as $hexColor) {
   351	                $variantCount++;
   352	                
   353	                Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Creating variant combination', [
   354	                    'combination' => "{$variantCount}/{$totalCombinations}",
   355	                    'size' => $size,
   356	                    'hex_color' => $hexColor
   357	                ]);
   358	
   359	                    try {
   360	
   361	                        // Create or find the attribute values
   362	                        $variantSize = VariantSize::firstOrCreate(['name' => $size]);
   363	                        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Variant size processed', [
   364	                            'size_id' => $variantSize->id,
   365	                            'size_name' => $variantSize->name,
   366	                            'was_created' => $variantSize->wasRecentlyCreated
   367	                        ]);
   368	
   369	                        $variantColor = VariantColor::firstOrCreate([
   370	                            'name' => $hexColor,
   371	                            'hex_code' => $hexColor,
   372	                            'description' => 'Extracted from image',
   373	                        ]);
   374	                        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Variant color processed', [
   375	                            'color_id' => $variantColor->id,
   376	                            'color_hex' => $variantColor->hex_code,
   377	                            'was_created' => $variantColor->wasRecentlyCreated
   378	                        ]);
   379	
   380	
   381	
   382	                        // Generate SKU
   383	                        $generatedSku = $this->generateSku($stock, $size, $hexColor);
   384	                        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Generated SKU', [
   385	                            'sku' => $generatedSku
   386	                        ]);
   387	
   388	                        // Create the variant
   389	                        $variant = new ProductVariant([
   390	                            'stock_id' => $stock->id,
   391	                            'price' => $variantPrice,
   392	                            'quantity' => $request->stock_quantity,
   393	                            'sku' => $generatedSku,
   394	                            'name' => "{$stock->product_name} - {$size}",
   395	                        ]);
   396	                        
   397	                        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - About to save variant', [
   398	                            'variant_data' => [
   399	                                'stock_id' => $variant->stock_id,
   400	                                'price' => $variant->price,
   401	                                'quantity' => $variant->quantity,
   402	                                'sku' => $variant->sku,
   403	                                'name' => $variant->name
   404	                            ]
   405	                        ]);
   406	
   407	                        $variant->save();
   408	
   409	                        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Variant saved successfully', [
   410	                            'variant_id' => $variant->id,
   411	                            'variant_sku' => $variant->sku,
   412	                            'variant_name' => $variant->name
   413	                        ]);
   414	
   415	                        // Attach attributes to the variant
   416	                        $attributeData = [
   417	                            'variant_id' => $variant->id,
   418	                            'size_id' => $variantSize->id,
   419	                            'color_id' => $variantColor->id,
   420	                            'created_at' => now(),
   421	                            'updated_at' => now(),
   422	                        ];
   423	                        
   424	                        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Inserting variant attributes', [
   425	                            'attribute_data' => $attributeData
   426	                        ]);
   427	
   428	                        DB::table('variant_attribute_values')->insert($attributeData);
   429	
   430	                        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Variant attributes inserted successfully');
   431	
   432	                        // Attach the image to the variant
   433	                        $imageAttachment = [
   434	                            'variant_id' => $variant->id,
   435	                            'image_id' => $productImage->id,
   436	                            'is_primary' => true,
   437	                            'sort_order' => 0,
   438	                            'created_at' => now(),
   439	                            'updated_at' => now(),
   440	                        ];
   441	
   442	                        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Inserting image attachment', [
   443	                            'image_attachment' => $imageAttachment
   444	                        ]);
   445	
   446	                        DB::table('variant_images')->insert($imageAttachment);
   447	
   448	                        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Image attachment inserted successfully', [
   449	                            'variant_id' => $variant->id,
   450	                            'image_id' => $productImage->id
   451	                        ]);
   452	
   453	                        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Variant creation completed for combination', [
   454	                            'combination' => "{$variantCount}/{$totalCombinations}",
   455	                            'variant_id' => $variant->id
   456	                        ]);
   457	
   458	                    } catch (\Exception $e) {
   459	                        Log::error('ProductImageController::createVariants - Failed to create variant', [
   460	                            'error_message' => $e->getMessage(),
   461	                            'error_file' => $e->getFile(),
   462	                            'error_line' => $e->getLine(),
   463	                            'error_trace' => $e->getTraceAsString(),
   464	                            'combination' => "{$variantCount}/{$totalCombinations}",
   465	                            'size' => $size,
   466	                            'hex_color' => $hexColor,
   467	                            'stock_id' => $stock->id
   468	                        ]);
   469	                        
   470	                        // Continue with next combination instead of failing completely
   471	                        continue;
   472	                    }
   473	                }
   474	        }
   475	
   476	        Log::info('ProductImageController::createVariants - Variant creation process completed', [
   477	            'total_combinations_processed' => $variantCount,
   478	            'expected_combinations' => $totalCombinations,
   479	            'stock_id' => $stock->id
   480	        ]);
   481	    }
   482

   520	                    'size' => $size,

     1	/**
     2	 * product-manage.js — Unified Admin Product Management
     3	 *
     4	 * Responsibilities:
     5	 *   1. Gallery image preview for multi-file input (#gallery-images-input)
     6	 *   2. Variant modal: open/close, prefill for edit, empty for create
     7	 *   3. Attribute-pair rows: add / remove (uniquely indexed)
     8	 *   4. Inventory inline PATCH via fetch() with CSRF + success tick
     9	 *
    10	 * Rules:
    11	 *   - Vanilla JS only, no framework.
    12	 *   - All dynamic URLs come from data-* attributes set in Blade.
    13	 *   - CSRF token read from <meta name="csrf-token">.
    14	 *   - RTL-safe: no direction assumptions in logic.
    15	 *   - 44 px touch targets are enforced in CSS (Blade side); JS does not break them.
    16	 */
    17	
    18	(function () {
    19	    'use strict';
    20	
    21	    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
    22	    /* Helpers                                                              */
    23	    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
    24	
    25	    function csrfToken() {
    26	        var meta = document.querySelector('meta[name="csrf-token"]');
    27	        return meta ? meta.getAttribute('content') : '';
    28	    }
    29	
    30	    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
    31	    /* 1. Gallery image preview                                             */
    32	    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
    33	
    34	    var galleryInput   = document.getElementById('gallery-images-input');
    35	    var galleryPreview = document.getElementById('gallery-preview');
    36	
    37	    if (galleryInput && galleryPreview) {
    38	        galleryInput.addEventListener('change', function () {
    39	            galleryPreview.innerHTML = '';
    40	
    41	            var files = Array.from(this.files);
    42	
    43	            if (files.length === 0) {
    44	                galleryPreview.classList.add('tw-hidden');
    45	                return;
    46	            }
    47	
    48	            galleryPreview.classList.remove('tw-hidden');
    49	
    50	            files.forEach(function (file) {
    51	                if (!file.type.startsWith('image/')) { return; }
    52	
    53	                var reader = new FileReader();
    54	                reader.onload = function (e) {
    55	                    var wrap = document.createElement('div');
    56	                    wrap.className = 'tw-relative tw-aspect-square tw-rounded-xl tw-overflow-hidden tw-border tw-border-indigo-100 tw-bg-slate-50';
    57	
    58	                    var img = document.createElement('img');
    59	                    img.src       = e.target.result;
    60	                    img.className = 'tw-w-full tw-h-full tw-object-cover';
    61	                    img.alt       = file.name;
    62	                    wrap.appendChild(img);
    63	
    64	                    var caption = document.createElement('span');
    65	                    caption.className = 'tw-absolute tw-bottom-0 tw-inset-x-0 tw-bg-black/60 tw-text-white tw-text-[10px] tw-px-2 tw-py-0.5 tw-truncate';
    66	                    caption.textContent = file.name;
    67	                    wrap.appendChild(caption);
    68	
    69	                    galleryPreview.appendChild(wrap);
    70	                };
    71	                reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    72	            });
    73	        });
    74	    }
    75	
    76	    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
    77	    /* 2. Variant modal                                                     */
    78	    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

    80	    var modal      = document.getElementById('variant-modal');

    82	    var modalTitle = document.getElementById('variant-modal-title');
    83	    var modalMethod = document.getElementById('variant-modal-method');
    84	
    85	    // Field refs
    86	    var vmName      = document.getElementById('vm-name');
    87	    var vmSku       = document.getElementById('vm-sku');
    88	    var vmPrice     = document.getElementById('vm-price');

    94	    var btnClose        = document.getElementById('btn-close-variant-modal');
    95	    var btnCancel       = document.getElementById('btn-cancel-variant-modal');
    96	
    97	    function openModal(mode, data) {
    98	        if (!modal || !modalForm) { return; }
    99	
   100	        // Reset attr pairs
   101	        renderAttrPairs([]);
   102	
   103	        if (mode === 'create') {
   104	            modalTitle.textContent = btnAddVariant
   105	                ? (btnAddVariant.textContent.trim())
   106	                : 'Add Variant';
   107	            modalMethod.value      = 'POST';
   108	            modalForm.action       = btnAddVariant
   109	                ? btnAddVariant.getAttribute('data-store-url')
   110	                : '';
   111	            // clear fields
   112	            if (vmName)      vmName.value      = '';
   113	            if (vmSku)       vmSku.value       = '';
   114	            if (vmPrice)     vmPrice.value     = '';
   115	            if (vmQuantity)  vmQuantity.value  = '';
   116	            if (vmIsActive)  vmIsActive.checked  = true;
   117	            if (vmIsDefault) vmIsDefault.checked = false;
   118	
   119	        } else {
   120	            // edit
   121	            modalTitle.textContent  = data.name || '';
   122	            modalMethod.value       = 'PUT';
   123	            modalForm.action        = data.updateUrl || '';
   124	            if (vmName)      vmName.value      = data.name      || '';
   125	            if (vmSku)       vmSku.value       = data.sku       || '';
   126	            if (vmPrice)     vmPrice.value     = data.price     || '';
   127	            if (vmQuantity)  vmQuantity.value  = data.quantity  || '';
   128	            if (vmIsActive)  vmIsActive.checked  = data.isActive  === '1';
   129	            if (vmIsDefault) vmIsDefault.checked = data.isDefault === '1';
   130	
   131	            // Attributes: decoded_attributes is a plain object {key: val}
   132	            var attrs = [];
   133	            if (data.attributes) {
   134	                try {
   135	                    var parsed = JSON.parse(data.attributes);
   136	                    if (typeof parsed === 'object' && !Array.isArray(parsed)) {
   137	                        attrs = Object.entries(parsed).map(function (kv) {
   138	                            return { key: kv[0], val: kv[1] };
   139	                        });
   140	                    }
   141	                } catch (err) { /* keep empty */ }
   142	            }
   143	            renderAttrPairs(attrs);
   144	        }
   145	
   146	        modal.classList.remove('tw-hidden');
   147	        modal.classList.add('tw-flex');
   148	        document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
   149	    }
   150	
   151	    function closeModal() {
   152	        if (!modal) { return; }
   153	        modal.classList.add('tw-hidden');
   154	        modal.classList.remove('tw-flex');
   155	        document.body.style.overflow = '';
   156	    }
   157	
   158	    // Open for create
   159	    if (btnAddVariant) {

   189	            if (e.target === modal) { closeModal(); }

   191	    }

   200	    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */

   202	    var attrPairsContainer = document.getElementById('attr-pairs');
   203	    var attrIndex = 0; // unique counter
   204	
   205	    function attrRowHtml(idx, keyVal, valVal) {
   206	        keyVal = keyVal || '';
   207	        valVal = valVal || '';
   208	        return '<div class="tw-flex tw-items-center tw-gap-2" id="attr-row-' + idx + '">'
   209	            + '<input type="text" name="attribute_keys[]" value="' + escapeHtml(keyVal) + '"'
   210	            + ' placeholder="' + 'Key' + '"'
   211	            + ' class="tw-flex-1 tw-rounded-xl tw-border tw-border-indigo-100 tw-bg-white tw-text-slate-800 tw-text-sm tw-px-3 tw-py-2 tw-shadow-sm focus:tw-outline-none focus:tw-border-amber-400 focus:tw-ring-2 focus:tw-ring-amber-100 tw-transition">'
   212	            + '<input type="text" name="attribute_values[]" value="' + escapeHtml(valVal) + '"'
   213	            + ' placeholder="' + 'Value' + '"'
   214	            + ' class="tw-flex-1 tw-rounded-xl tw-border tw-border-indigo-100 tw-bg-white tw-text-slate-800 tw-text-sm tw-px-3 tw-py-2 tw-shadow-sm focus:tw-outline-none focus:tw-border-amber-400 focus:tw-ring-2 focus:tw-ring-amber-100 tw-transition">'
   215	            + '<button type="button" data-remove="' + idx + '"'
   216	            + ' class="tw-w-8 tw-h-8 tw-rounded-full tw-bg-rose-50 hover:tw-bg-rose-100 tw-text-rose-600 tw-flex tw-items-center tw-justify-center tw-transition tw-flex-shrink-0"'
   217	            + ' aria-label="Remove">'
   218	            + '<i class="la la-times tw-text-sm"></i>'
   219	            + '</button>'
   220	            + '</div>';
   221	    }
   222	
   223	    function renderAttrPairs(pairs) {
   224	        if (!attrPairsContainer) { return; }
   225	        attrPairsContainer.innerHTML = '';
   226	        attrIndex = 0;
   227	
   228	        if (!pairs || pairs.length === 0) {
   229	            addAttrRow('', '');
   230	            return;
   231	        }
   232	        pairs.forEach(function (pair) {
   233	            addAttrRow(pair.key, pair.val);
   234	        });
   235	    }
   236	
   237	    function addAttrRow(keyVal, valVal) {
   238	        if (!attrPairsContainer) { return; }
   239	        var idx = attrIndex++;
   240	        var div = document.createElement('div');
   241	        div.innerHTML = attrRowHtml(idx, keyVal, valVal);
   242	        var row = div.firstChild;
   243	        attrPairsContainer.appendChild(row);
   244	    }
   245	
   246	    // Add button
   247	    var btnAddAttr = document.getElementById('btn-add-attr');
   248	    if (btnAddAttr) {
   249	        btnAddAttr.addEventListener('click', function () {
   250	            addAttrRow('', '');
   251	        });
   252	    }
   253	
   254	    // Remove row (delegated)
   255	    if (attrPairsContainer) {
   256	        attrPairsContainer.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
   257	            var btn = e.target.closest('[data-remove]');
   258	            if (!btn) { return; }
   259	            var idx = btn.getAttribute('data-remove');
   260	            var row = document.getElementById('attr-row-' + idx);
   261	            if (row) {
   262	                // Always keep at least one row
   263	                var allRows = attrPairsContainer.querySelectorAll('[id^="attr-row-"]');
   264	                if (allRows.length > 1) {
   265	                    row.remove();
   266	                } else {
   267	                    // Clear values but keep the row
   268	                    row.querySelectorAll('input').forEach(function (inp) { inp.value = ''; });
   269	                }
   270	            }
   271	        });
   272	    }
   273	
   274	    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
   275	    /* 4. Inventory inline PATCH                                            */
   276	    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
   277	
   278	    document.querySelectorAll('.btn-inv-save').forEach(function (btn) {
   279	        btn.addEventListener('click', function () {
   280	            var variantId = btn.getAttribute('data-variant-id');
   281	            var url       = btn.getAttribute('data-url');
   282	            var row       = document.querySelector('[data-inventory-row="' + variantId + '"]');
   283	
   284	            if (!row || !url) { return; }
   285	
   286	            var qtyInput   = row.querySelector('.inv-qty');
   287	            var priceInput = row.querySelector('.inv-price');
   288	            var tick       = row.querySelector('.inv-tick');
   289	
   290	            var quantity = qtyInput   ? parseFloat(qtyInput.value)   : null;
   291	            var price    = priceInput ? parseFloat(priceInput.value)  : null;
   292	
   293	            if (quantity === null || price === null || isNaN(quantity) || isNaN(price)) {
   294	                return;
   295	            }
   296	
   297	            btn.disabled = true;
   298	            btn.style.opacity = '0.6';
   299	
   300	            fetch(url, {
   301	                method  : 'PATCH',
   302	                headers : {
   303	                    'Content-Type'  : 'application/json',
   304	                    'Accept'        : 'application/json',
   305	                    'X-CSRF-TOKEN'  : csrfToken(),
   306	                },
   307	                body : JSON.stringify({ quantity: quantity, price: price }),
   308	            })
   309	            .then(function (res) {
   310	                if (!res.ok) { throw new Error('HTTP ' + res.status); }
   311	                return res.json();
   312	            })
   313	            .then(function (data) {
   314	                btn.disabled = false;
   315	                btn.style.opacity = '';
   316	
   317	                if (tick) {
   318	                    tick.classList.remove('tw-hidden');
   319	                    setTimeout(function () {
   320	                        tick.classList.add('tw-hidden');
   321	                    }, 2500);
   322	                }
   323	            })
   324	            .catch(function (err) {
   325	                btn.disabled = false;
   326	                btn.style.opacity = '';
   327	                console.error('Inventory update failed:', err);
   328	            });
   329	        });
   330	    });
   331	
   332	    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
   333	    /* Utility                                                              */
   334	    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
   335	
   336	    function escapeHtml(str) {
   337	        if (str == null) { return ''; }
   338	        return String(str)
   339	            .replace(/&/g,  '&amp;')
   340	            .replace(/</g,  '&lt;')
   341	            .replace(/>/g,  '&gt;')
   342	            .replace(/"/g,  '&quot;')
   343	            .replace(/'/g,  '&#039;');
   344	    }
   345	
   346	})();

   584	                            'size_id' => $variantSize->id,
   585	                            'color_id' => $variantColor->id,
   586	                            'created_at' => now(),
   587	                            'updated_at' => now(),
   588	                        ];
   589	                        
   590	                        \Log::info('ProductImageController::createGroupVariants - Inserting variant attributes', [
   591	                            'attribute_data' => $attributeData
   592	                        ]);
   593	
   594	                        DB::table('variant_attribute_values')->insert($attributeData);
   595	
   596	                        \Log::info('ProductImageController::createGroupVariants - Variant attributes inserted successfully');
   597	
   598	                        // Attach all images to this variant
   599	                        $imageAttachments = [];
   600	                        foreach ($productImages as $index => $productImage) {
   601	                            $imageAttachments[] = [
   602	                                'variant_id' => $variant->id,
   603	                                'image_id' => $productImage->id,
   604	                                'is_primary' => ($index === 0), // First image is primary for this variant
   605	                                'sort_order' => $index,
   606	                                'created_at' => now(),
   607	                                'updated_at' => now(),
   608	                            ];
   609	                        }
   610	
   611	                        \Log::info('ProductImageController::createGroupVariants - Preparing image attachments', [
   612	                            'variant_id' => $variant->id,
   613	                            'image_attachments_count' => count($imageAttachments),
   614	                            'image_attachments' => $imageAttachments
   615	                        ]);
   616	
   617	                        // Bulk insert all image attachments
   618	                        if (! empty($imageAttachments)) {
   619	                            DB::table('variant_images')->insert($imageAttachments);
   620	                            \Log::info('ProductImageController::createGroupVariants - Image attachments inserted successfully', [
   621	                                'variant_id' => $variant->id,
   622	                                'attachments_count' => count($imageAttachments)
   623	                            ]);
   624	                        }
   625	
   626	                        \Log::info('ProductImageController::createGroupVariants - Variant creation completed for combination', [
   627	                            'combination' => "{$variantCount}/{$totalCombinations}",
   628	                            'variant_id' => $variant->id
   629	                        ]);
   630	
   631	                    } catch (\Exception $e) {
   632	                        \Log::error('ProductImageController::createGroupVariants - Failed to create variant', [
   633	                            'error_message' => $e->getMessage(),
   634	                            'error_file' => $e->getFile(),
   635	                            'error_line' => $e->getLine(),
   636	                            'error_trace' => $e->getTraceAsString(),
   637	                            'combination' => "{$variantCount}/{$totalCombinations}",
   638	                            'size' => $size,
   639	                            'hex_color' => $hexColor,
   640	                            'stock_id' => $stock->id
   641	                        ]);
   642	                        
   643	                        // Continue with next combination instead of failing completely
   644	                        continue;
   645	                    }
   646	                }
   647	        }
   648	
   649	        \Log::info('ProductImageController::createGroupVariants - Group variant creation process completed', [
   650	            'total_variants_created' => count($createdVariants),
   651	            'expected_variants' => $totalCombinations,
   652	            'stock_id' => $stock->id
   653	        ]);
   654	
   655	        return $createdVariants;
   656	    }
   657	
   658	    /**
   659	     * Update the specified image.
   660	     */
   661	    public function update(Request $request, Stock $stock_id, ProductImage $image)
   662	    {
   663	        // Rename variable to match expected name in views
   664	        $stock = $stock_id;
   665	        Log::info($request->all());
   666	        $request->validate([
   667	            'alt_text' => 'nullable|string|max:255',
   668	            'sort_order' => 'nullable|integer|min:0',
   669	            'sizes' => 'required|array',
   670	            'sizes.*' => 'required|string',
   671	            'selected_colors' => 'required|array',
   672	            'selected_colors.*' => 'required|string',
   673	            'variant_price' => 'required|numeric|min:0',
   674	            'stock_quantity' => 'required|integer|min:0',
   675	        ]);
   676	        Log::info($request->all());
   677	        try {
   678	
   679	            DB::beginTransaction();
   680	
   681	            // Update basic image information
   682	            $image->update($request->only(['alt_text', 'sort_order']));
   683	
   684	            // Get existing variants for this image
   685	            $existingVariants = $image->variants()->pluck('id')->toArray();
   686	
   687	            // Create or update variants for each combination
   688	            foreach ($request->sizes as $size) {
   689	                foreach ($request->selected_colors as $color) {
   690	                    // Check if variant already exists
   691	                    $variant = ProductVariant::firstOrNew([
   692	                        'stock_id' => $stock->id,
   693	                        'size' => $size,
   694	                        'color' => $color,
   695	                    ]);
   696	
   697	                    // Update or set variant details
   698	                    $variant->price = $request->variant_price;
   699	                    $variant->quantity = $request->stock_quantity;
   700	                    if (! $variant->exists) {
   701	                        $variant->sku = $this->generateSku($stock, $size, $color);
   702	                    }
   703	                    $variant->save();
   704	
   705	                        // Attach image to variant if not already attached
   706	                        if (! $image->variants->contains($variant->id)) {
   707	                            $image->variants()->attach($variant->id, [
   708	                                'sort_order' => $variant->images()->max('pivot_sort_order') + 1,
   709	                            ]);
   710	                        }
   711	
   712	                        // Remove from existing variants array
   713	                        $key = array_search($variant->id, $existingVariants);
   714	                        if ($key !== false) {
   715	                            unset($existingVariants[$key]);
   716	                        }
   717	                }
   718	            }
   719	
   720	            // Detach any variants that are no longer selected
   721	            if (! empty($existingVariants)) {
   722	                $image->variants()->detach($existingVariants);
   723	            }
   724	
   725	            DB::commit();
   726	
   727	            return response()->json([
   728	                'success' => true,
   729	                'message' => 'Image and variants updated successfully',
   730	                'image' => $image->load('variants'),
   731	            ]);
   732	
   733	        } catch (\Exception $e) {
   734	            DB::rollBack();
   735	
   736	            return response()->json([
   737	                'success' => false,
   738	                'message' => 'Failed to update image: '.$e->getMessage(),
   739	            ], 500);
   740	        }
   741	    }
   742	
   743	    /**
   744	     * Set an image as primary for a product or variant.
   745	     */
   746	    public function setPrimary(Request $request, Stock $stock_id, ProductImage $image)
   747	    {
   748	        // Rename variable to match expected name in views
   749	        $stock = $stock_id;
   750	
   751	        try {
   752	            // Get the stock ID from the image
   753	            $stockId = $image->stock_id;
   754	
   755	            // First set all images of this stock to non-primary (0)
   756	            ProductImage::where('stock_id', $stockId)
   757	                ->update(['is_primary' => 0]);
   758	
   759	            // Then set the selected image as primary (1)
   760	            $image->is_primary = 1;
   761	            $image->save();
   762	
   763	            // Update the stock's image_id to point to this image
   764	            Stock::where('id', $stockId)->update(['image_id' => $image->id]);
   765	
   766	            return redirect()->back()
   767	                ->with('success', __('messages.primary_image_set'));
   768	
   769	        } catch (\Exception $e) {
   770	            return redirect()->back()
   771	                ->with('error', __('messages.failed_to_set_primary'));
   772	        }
   773	    }
   774	
   775	    /**
   776	     * Set an image as primary for a specific color group.
   777	     */
   778	    public function setGroupPrimary(Request $request, Stock $stock_id, ProductImage $image)
   779	    {
   780	        // Rename variable to match expected name in views
   781	        $stock = $stock_id;
   782	
   783	        try {
   784	            // Get the stock ID and color group from the image
   785	            $stockId = $image->stock_id;
   786	            $colorGroup = $image->color_group;
   787	
   788	            if (! $colorGroup) {
   789	                // If no color group, assign one
   790	                $colorGroup = 'group_'.time();
   791	                $image->color_group = $colorGroup;
   792	                $image->save();
   793	            }
   794	
   795	            // First reset all group primary flags for this color group
   796	            ProductImage::where('stock_id', $stockId)
   797	                ->where('color_group', $colorGroup)
   798	                ->update(['is_group_primary' => 0]);
   799	
   800	            // Set the selected image as primary for this color group
   801	            $image->is_group_primary = 1;
   802	            $image->color_hex = $image->color_hex ?? '#000000';
   803	            $image->save();
   804	
   805	            // Store this image as the primary for its color group in the database
   806	            DB::table('product_color_groups')->updateOrInsert(
   807	                ['stock_id' => $stockId, 'color_group' => $colorGroup],
   808	                ['primary_image_id' => $image->id, 'updated_at' => now()]
   809	            );
   810	
   811	            return redirect()->back()
   812	                ->with('success', "Primary image set for color group: {$colorGroup}");
   813	
   814	        } catch (\Exception $e) {
   815	            Log::error('Error setting group primary image: '.$e->getMessage());
   816	
   817	            return redirect()->back()
   818	                ->with('error', 'Failed to set primary image for color group: '.$e->getMessage());
   819	        }
   820	    }
   821	
   822	    /**
   823	     * Remove the specified image from storage.
   824	     */
   825	    public function destroy(Request $request, Stock $stock_id, ProductImage $image)
   826	    {
   827	        // Rename variable to match expected name in views
   828	        $stock = $stock_id;
   829	
   830	        try {
   831	            // Delete the physical file
   832	            if ($image->image_path && Storage::exists($image->image_path)) {
   833	                Storage::delete($image->image_path);
   834	            }
   835	
   836	            // If this was the primary image, make another image primary
   837	            if ($image->is_primary) {
   838	                $nextImage = $stock->productImages()
   839	                    ->where('id', '!=', $image->id)
   840	                    ->first();
   841	                if ($nextImage) {
   842	                    $nextImage->update(['is_primary' => 1]);
   843	                }
   844	            }
   845	
   846	            // Delete the database record
   847	            $image->delete();
   848	
   849	            if ($request->filled('redirect_to') && str_starts_with($request->input('redirect_to'), url('/'))) {
   850	                return redirect($request->input('redirect_to'))->with('success', __('messages.image_deleted'));
   851	            }
   852	
   853	            return redirect()->route('stocks.index')->with('success', __('messages.image_deleted'));
   854	
   855	        } catch (\Exception $e) {
   856	            return redirect()->route('stocks.index')->with('error', __('messages.failed_to_delete_image'));
   857	        }
   858	    }
   859	
   860	    /**
   861	     * Generate a unique SKU for the product variant
   862	     */
   863	    private function generateSku(Stock $stock, string $size, string $hexColor): string
   864	    {
   865	        $baseCode = Str::slug(Str::substr($stock->product_name, 0, 3));
   866	        $colorCode = Str::substr(str_replace('#', '', $hexColor), 0, 3);
   867	        $sizeCode = $size;
   868	        $random = Str::random(2);
   869	
   870	        return Str::upper("{$baseCode}-{$colorCode}-{$sizeCode}-{$random}");
   871	    }
   872	}

    25	
    26	class LanguageService
    27	{
    28	    private $defaultLocale = 'ar';
    29	
    30	    const SUPPORTED_LOCALES = ['ar', 'ma', 'en', 'fr', 'es'];
    31	
    32	    public function __construct()
    33	    {
    34	        // Don't force Arabic locale on initialization - let middleware handle it
    35	        // We'll use the locale set by the middleware or fall back to config default
    36	    }
    37	
    38	    public function getActiveLocale(): string
    39	    {
    40	        // Get locale from URL segment
    41	        $locale = request()->segment(1);
    42	
    43	        // Check if it's a valid locale
    44	        if (in_array($locale, self::SUPPORTED_LOCALES)) {
    45	            return $locale;
    46	        }
    47	
    48	        // Fallback to Laravel's current locale
    49	        return App::getLocale();
    50	    }
    51	
    52	    public function resolveLocalizedFieldName(string $field, array $locales = self::SUPPORTED_LOCALES): string
    53	    {
    54	        $activeLocale = $this->getActiveLocale();
    55	
    56	        return in_array($activeLocale, $locales)
    57	            ? "{$field}_{$activeLocale}"
    58	            : "{$field}_{$this->defaultLocale}";
    59	    }
    60	
    61	    /**
    62	     * Share language and user data with all views
    63	     */
    64	    public function shareLang()
    65	    {
    66	        $user = Auth::user();
    67	        View::share(['lang' => $this->getActiveLocale(), 'user' => $user]);
    68	    }
    69	
    70	    /**
    71	     * Get the translated value from a model's localized fields
    72	     */
    73	    public function resolveTranslation(?Model $model, string $baseField): string
    74	    {
    75	        // Check if the model is null
    76	        if (is_null($model)) {
    77	            return '';
    78	        }
    79	
    80	        $activeLocale = $this->getActiveLocale();
    81	
    82	        // Define fallback chain based on active locale
    83	        if ($activeLocale === 'ma') {
    84	            $fallbackLocale = 'ar'; // Moroccan Darija falls back to Standard Arabic
    85	        } elseif ($activeLocale === 'ar') {
    86	            $fallbackLocale = 'ma'; // Arabic falls back to Moroccan Darija
    87	        } else {
    88	            $fallbackLocale = 'ar'; // All other languages fall back to Arabic
    89	        }
    90	
    91	        $primaryField = "{$baseField}_{$activeLocale}";
    92	        $fallbackField = "{$baseField}_{$fallbackLocale}";
    93	
    94	        // First try the active locale
    95	        if (! empty($model->{$primaryField})) {
    96	            return $model->{$primaryField};
    97	        }
    98	
    99	        // If active locale is empty, try the fallback locale
   100	        if (! empty($model->{$fallbackField})) {
   101	            return $model->{$fallbackField};
   102	        }
   103	
   104	        // If both are empty, try getting any non-empty localized field
   105	        foreach (self::SUPPORTED_LOCALES as $locale) {
   106	            $field = "{$baseField}_{$locale}";
   107	            if (! empty($model->{$field})) {
   108	                return $model->{$field};
   109	            }
   110	        }
   111	
   112	        return ''; // Return empty string if no translation found in any locale
   113	    }
   114	
   115	    /**
   116	     * Get all translated model fields
   117	     */
   118	    public function resolveAllTranslations(): array
   119	    {
   120	        $translations = [];

- [ProductVariantController.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Http/Controllers/Admin/ProductVariantController.php:64), [ProductImageController.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Http/Controllers/Admin/ProductImageController.php:487), [CategoryProductsController.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Http/Controllers/API/Frontend/CategoryProductsController.php:199) - P0 - Variant attributes have no canonical source: seller/manage flows write free-form JSON, image flow writes pivots, and storefront still treats pivots as primary. Suggested fix: make `product_variants.attributes` the only writable source, backfill it from existing pivot rows, switch storefront reads to JSON first/only, and keep lookup/pivot tables only as derived projections if you still need faceting.

- [ProductVariantController.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Http/Controllers/Admin/ProductVariantController.php:97), [ProductVariantController.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Http/Controllers/Admin/ProductVariantController.php:166) - P0 - The same `variant_attribute_values` table is written two incompatible ways: `attach()` creates partial size/color/fabric rows, while update assumes one row containing all three IDs. Suggested fix: stop using three `attach()` calls on this table; either write one normalized attribute row per variant through a dedicated model/service, or stop writing pivots entirely once JSON is canonical.

- [index.blade.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/resources/views/admin/products/manage/index.blade.php:37), [index.blade.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/resources/views/admin/products/manage/index.blade.php:425), [StockController.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Http/Controllers/Admin/StockController.php:254), [ProductVariantController.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Http/Controllers/Admin/ProductVariantController.php:131) - P0 - The unified page composition is fine in principle, but the current forms post payloads that the reused controllers do not actually accept: basics sends bilingual fields to a locale-driven action, and the variant modal sends attribute pairs to an update action that requires lookup IDs. Suggested fix: keep the normal-form + PRG approach, but add section-specific “manage” endpoints/request DTOs that adapt the page payload into one shared domain service; do not reuse legacy actions whose contracts differ.

- [CategoryProductsController.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Http/Controllers/API/Frontend/CategoryProductsController.php:173), [CategoryProductsController.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Http/Controllers/API/Frontend/CategoryProductsController.php:236), [Stock.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Models/Stock.php:317), [ProductVariantController.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Http/Controllers/Admin/ProductVariantController.php:295) - P0 - Availability is still keyed off `stocks.quantity` or a 300s cached `total_quantity`, and most variant write paths do not invalidate that cache. Suggested fix: remove the accessor cache or replace it with `withSum/loadSum` on active variants, and base storefront filtering plus `in_stock` on variant quantity with `stocks.quantity` only as a no-variant fallback.

- [ProductVariantController.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Http/Controllers/Admin/ProductVariantController.php:79), [ProductVariant.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Models/ProductVariant.php:24), [ProductVariant.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Models/ProductVariant.php:140) - P1 - JSON attribute handling is internally inconsistent: store manually `json_encode`s into a JSON-cast column, the accessor decodes raw storage directly, and update/image flows do not keep JSON synchronized. Suggested fix: always assign arrays, never pre-encode; make `decoded_attributes` read the casted attribute; route every variant write through one serializer/normalizer.

- [Seller/ProductController.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Http/Controllers/Seller/ProductController.php:111), [CategoryProductsController.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Http/Controllers/API/Frontend/CategoryProductsController.php:157), [StockController.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Http/Controllers/Admin/StockController.php:256) - P1 - Product text fields are not coherent: seller writes `description`, storefront selects `description_en`, and admin basics update only persists the locale-specific field chosen from the URL. Suggested fix: pick one explicit bilingual schema for stock text fields, backfill it, and make both seller/admin writers always persist both language columns.

- [StockController.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Http/Controllers/Admin/StockController.php:59), [Stock.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Models/Stock.php:277), [stock_table.blade.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/resources/views/admin/includes/stocks/stock_table.blade.php:77) - P1 - The stock list has avoidable N+1s: it does not eager-load images but every row calls `image_url`, while the super-admin branch eagerly loads `variants` even though the table does not use them. Suggested fix: load `primaryImage`/`productImages` explicitly for the list, drop unused `variants` eager-loading there, and use explicit aggregate columns instead of accessor side effects.

- [ProductImageController.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Http/Controllers/Admin/ProductImageController.php:556), [ProductImageController.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Http/Controllers/Admin/ProductImageController.php:863), [ProductVariantController.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Http/Controllers/Admin/ProductVariantController.php:181) - P1 - Variant naming/SKU generation relies on `$stock->product_name`, which `Stock` does not define, so image-created or admin-renamed variants can get malformed names/SKUs. Suggested fix: add one explicit stock display-name helper and use that everywhere variant names/SKUs are composed.

- [ProductManagementController.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Http/Controllers/Admin/ProductManagementController.php:50), [routes/api.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/routes/api.php:439), [Stock.php](/Users/mohamedbardouni/projects/beldify/beldify-backend/app/Models/Stock.php:24) - P2 - The admin product API is a third writer with a different field/storage contract from the Blade controllers, and some of its mass-assigned fields do not align with `Stock::$fillable`. Suggested fix: freeze these routes until the shared product write service exists, or rewrite them to call the same service/storage path as seller/admin.

Single most important change: make `product_variants.attributes` the only writable source of variant attributes, then force every seller/admin/storefront path through one normalizer/service that reads and writes that schema.
